# Progress tracker

Tracks feature units per the workflow in `CLAUDE.md`. One section per unit.

> **Older history is archived.** Units before Spec 21 live in [`progress-archive.md`](progress-archive.md), kept out of this file to save context. This file holds Spec 21 onward.

## Spec 146 U3 - equipment usage logs: check-out/check-in Б├▓ per-WP charge Б├▓ wp_profit (ADR 0055 + ADR 0060 б╖2) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-20** (commits ba8a52d feat б╥ 115d6ab director-fix б╥ 6ed8af0 types; migrations 20260767000000Б─⌠000400). Closes the spec 161 U3b equipment gap (`equipment_cost=0`/`equipment_costed=false`): attribute equipment to a WP via a **check-out/check-in usage log**, derive a **per-WP equipment charge live**, wire into `wp_profit`. **Verify:** lintб╥typecheckб╥test **188/1268**б╥db:push (5 migrations)б╥db:types (app+worker)б╥**db:test 105 files (104 passed; my 105=41/41, 102/90/91/86 all green)** Б─■ the **1 failure is `104-settlement-engine.test.sql`, the CONCURRENT session's in-progress file, NOT mine** (its closed-project seed bug; not in any of my commits). **Operator picks (this session, via AskUserQuestion):** (1) granularity = **check-out Б├▓ check-in SPAN** (one row/checkout, billed whole days on site ц≈ daily rate), NOT row-per-day; (2) the WP is charged the **CHARGE-OUT daily rate computed LIVE** (transfer price, symmetric with DC labor @ SELL; PRC keeps the margin over the batch cost Б─■ Case A + ADR 0060 б╖2), NOT a GL-allocated batch-cost share. **This REVISES the roadmap-table U3/U4 sketch** (was per-day log + frozen `wp_equipment_costs`): the live `wp_profit` reuses live reads (`wp_labor_sell`), never the frozen snapshot, so the frozen `wp_equipment_costs`/`freeze_wp_equipment_cost` (old U4) is deferred to budget-vs-spend + a WP-dimensioned equipment GL posting (later seam). **No new GL account this unit** Б─■ the charge-out is a number the GL doesn't hold (GL holds batch COST at batch grain), so computing it live from the usage logs is the transfer-price layer, NOT a second costing path (exactly like `wp_labor_sell` vs the GL's labor COST).

**Builds:** `equipment_usage_logs` (append-only, supersede; `item_id`/`work_package_id` WP-grain/`checked_out_on`/`checked_in_on` null=open/`daily_rate_snapshot` MONEY zero-grant/`superseded_by`/`correction_reason` nullable Б─■ NO `reason-iff-superseded` CHECK since check-in is the first supersede; CHECK inБ┴╔out; column-scoped SELECT omitting the rate, like `labor_logs`; append-only block trigger) б╥ `check_out_equipment(item,wp,date)` (gate site_admin/pm/procurement/super; per-item advisory lock; item must be priced + WP not complete + no existing open checkout for the item Б├▓ P0001) б╥ `check_in_equipment(log,date)` (closes the open row via a superseding closed successor; in<out Б├▓ P0001; re-check-in of closed/superseded Б├▓ P0001) б╥ `wp_equipment_sell(p_wp)` (mirror `wp_labor_sell`: super+director gate null-safe, нё over CURRENT rows of `greatest((coalesce(checked_in_on,current_date)Б┬▓checked_out_on)+1,0) ц≈ daily_rate_snapshot` Б─■ whole days inclusive, open accrues to today, no internal/external branch) б╥ `wp_profit` REPLACE (same signature; `equipment_cost = wp_equipment_sell`, `equipment_costed = true`). pgTAP **file 105** (104 taken by a concurrent Spec 161 U4b settlement-engine session Б─■ renumbered; my migrations likewise 20260766Б├▓20260767 around their pushed settlement_engine) + update `102-wp-profit` (`equipment_costed` falseБ├▓true). Spec 146 U3 detail authored first.

**ADR 0058 fix (migration 20260767000400):** the check_out/check_in RPC gates + the `equipment_usage_logs` read policy initially named `project_manager` WITHOUT `project_director` Б├▓ **pgTAP 90 + 91 (the see-all-PM completeness invariants) caught it** on the first GREEN db:test. Forward-fix migration adds `project_director` to both gates + the policy (DROP+CREATE Б─■ no CREATE OR REPLACE POLICY). Lesson re-confirmed: **any new gate/policy naming project_manager must also name project_director** ([[spec152-project-director-role]]). **Concurrent-session reconciliation:** the half-applied push (table created but unrecorded after the 20260766 collision) was repaired via `supabase migration repair --status applied 20260767000000` then push-the-rest Б─■ NOT a re-create (verified table+fn+trigger+policy+grants all present first via `supabase db query`).

## Spec 161 U4a - settlement multiplier dial: nova_dials (ADR 0060 б╖3 + decision a) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-20.** Migration `20260765000000_settlement_multiplier_dial.sql`. Third unit this session (operator chose "build w/ seeded default" via AskUserQuestion). ADR 0060 б╖3: coin pool = нё banked WP profits ц≈ the **project multiplier** ("the most important undefined lever"). Per **build-decision (a)** (every dial = editable seeded data, tune anytime) the multiplier ships as a **seeded editable dial**, not a constant Б─■ the settlement engine (U4b) reads it. **`nova_dials`** = the one **key/value home for every economic dial** (the literal ADR-decision-a shape; HT cut % + level weights [U5] + saver-bonus rate [U6] land here as seeded rows in their units): `dial_key text PK`, `value numeric(20,4) Б┴╔0`, updated_by/at. **MONEY/economics posture: zero authenticated grant** (operator reads via admin client behind requireRole; U4b engine reads via definer; setter is sole writer). **Seeded `('coin_multiplier', 1.0)`** Б─■ placeholder (1 baht banked profit Б├▓ 1 coin point; coins=abstract points no peg, decision b); **operator MUST calibrate vs utilization before go-live** (standing markup-% open dial Б─■ flagged, not blocking: mechanism ships, number tuned). **`set_nova_dial(p_key,p_value)`** SECURITY DEFINER **super_admin-only** (operator economics, anti-favoritism б╖5, like sell-rate dials; null-safe `is distinct from`; **no PM ref Б├▓ 90/91 untouched**) Б├▓ 42501; valueБ┴╔0 (P0001); **update-only on a SEEDED key** (typo'd key Б├▓ P0001, no phantom dials); audits (generic `update` action, target nova_dials, payload key+old+new Б─■ no enum-add). **U4a = the dial ONLY**; the settlement math (нё wp_profit ц≈ multiplier Б├▓ pool) + banking-at-completion = **U4b**, mirrors U1-dials-before-U3-read.

**pgTAP 103** (13 asserts: catalog table+dial_key PK+value col+set_nova_dial secdef; seed coin_multiplier=1.0; money posture authenticated-no-SELECT; super tunes to 1.5 + reads back + audited once; negativeБ├▓P0001; unknown keyБ├▓P0001; pmб╥visitorБ├▓42501). Verify: lintб╥typecheckб╥test **188/1268**б╥db:pushб╥**db:test 103 files/1993/0** (was 1980 Б├▓ +13)б╥db:types (nova_dials + set_nova_dial added) Б─■ all green. **U4a spec detail authored first.** **NEXT = U4b settlement engine** (нё wp_profit over project WPs ц≈ coin_multiplier Б├▓ coin pool; banking profit at WP completion; null-budget WP handling) Б├▓ U5 distribution (HT cut + level weights Б├▓ `coin_postings`) Б├▓ U6 shop. **U4b/go-live STILL wants operator UTILIZATION DATA** to calibrate coin_multiplier (seeded 1.0 is a placeholder). LESSON: pnpm must run from the INNER nested repo (`prc-ops/prc-ops`) Б─■ bash cwd reset to outer mid-session, ERR_PNPM_NO_IMPORTER_MANIFEST_FOUND; cd inner or `pnpm -C prc-ops`.

## Spec 161 U3b - WP profit assembly: wp_profit, materials from GL (ADR 0060 б╖2 + ADR 0057) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-20.** Migration `20260764000000_wp_profit.sql`. Assembles the б╖2 read `profit = budget Б┬▓ labor_sell Б┬▓ materials Б┬▓ equipment`, **exposing every term** (returns table). **`wp_profit(p_wp uuid) returns table(budget, labor_sell, materials_cost, equipment_cost, equipment_costed, profit)`** SECURITY DEFINERб╥stableб╥pinned search_path. **budget** = wp_economics.budget (NULL until PD sets Б├▓ profit NULL). **labor_sell** = `wp_labor_sell(p_wp)` REUSED (definer-to-definer: caller's role resolves so its identical super/director gate passes Б─■ no re-impl). **materials_cost DERIVED FROM THE GL** (ADR 0057, NOT a re-sum of purchase_requests): `нё(debitБ┬▓credit)` on `journal_lines` for the WP on WIP account **1400**, restricted to PURCHASE-sourced entries via `coalesce(orig.source_table, e.source_table)='purchase_requests'` (`left join journal_entries orig on orig.id=e.reversal_of`) Б─■ **reversal-safe** (a reversal carries source_table 'journal_reversal' but copies work_package_id + swaps debit/credit, so an auto-corrected purchase nets via reversal_ofБ├▓original's source; verified `post_purchase_to_gl` reverse-and-reposts). **Labor also debits 1400 but EXCLUDED** (source wp_labor_costs); VAT (1300) + equipment (no WP dim) naturally excluded. **profit = budgetБ┬▓labor_sellБ┬▓materialsБ┬▓equipment, NULL if budget NULL.** Gate **super_admin+project_director** (no PM ref Б├▓ 90/91 untouched), null-safe `is distinct from` (NULL-role denied) Б├▓ 42501; unknown WP Б├▓ P0001; execute revoke-public/grant-authenticated; read Б├▓ no audit/enum.

**EQUIPMENT GAP (operator-confirmed via AskUserQuestion 2026-06-20 Б─■ chose "build profit w/o equipment, flag it"):** investigation (Explore agent + verified by hand) found `post_rental_batch_to_gl` ([20260743000100:176-178]) posts a rental batch to WIP 1400 at **batch grain with NO work_package_id (nor project_id)** Б─■ equipment cost is **not WP-dimensioned in the GL**, can't be derived per-WP today. Splitting a batch across a project's WPs needs a **business allocation rule** = a follow-up spec touching the equipment poster / ADR 0055 (operator decision). U3b does NOT improvise it (scope rule + "discovering a missing requirement mid-unit isn't license to expand"): **equipment_cost=0 + equipment_costed=false** so the omission is LOUD, never folded silently. U4 minting is blocked anyway Б├▓ no payout rides on the partial figure. Profit is OVERSTATED by missing equipment until that follow-up.

**pgTAP 102** (18 asserts: catalog has_function+secdef; gate super+director read / pmб╥saб╥visitor 42501; WP-A all 6 components [budget 5000б╥labor_sell 800б╥materials 1000 (labor 1400 entry EXCLUDED)б╥equipment 0б╥equipment_costed falseб╥profit 3200]; WP-B reversal-safe materials [2000Б┬▓2000+1500=1500, profit 2500]; WP-C budget-null Б├▓ budget NULL + profit NULL; unknown WP P0001). Journal rows seeded directly (accounting_period 2099-12 + journal_entries/lines, gl_accounts by code) to isolate from the poster machinery. Verify: lintб╥typecheckб╥test **188/1268**б╥db:pushб╥**db:test 102 files/1980/0** (was 1962 Б├▓ +18)б╥db:types (`wp_profit` added) Б─■ all green. **U3b spec detail authored first.** **NEXT = equipment-per-WP follow-up spec** (allocation rule, gated on operator basis) + **U4 settlement ц≈ project multiplier** (gated on utilization data for markup-%/multiplier). LESSONS: reversal entries carry source_table='journal_reversal' (not the original's) but COPY work_package_id + swap debit/credit Б├▓ net via reversal_ofБ├▓orig.source_table; labor + materials BOTH hit WIP 1400 Б├▓ must isolate by source, not account alone.

## Spec 161 U3 - WP labor priced at SELL: wp_labor_sell (ADR 0060 б╖2) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-20.** Migration `20260763000000_wp_labor_sell.sql`. The **novel core** of the б╖2 profit engine Б─■ `WP profit = budget Б┬▓ (equipment + DC labor @ SELL + materials)` Б─■ built as **only** the SELL-priced DC-labor term (the one number no existing fn produces; `freeze_wp_labor_cost` sums the same logs at COST). **`wp_labor_sell(p_wp uuid) returns numeric`** SECURITY DEFINER б╥ `stable` б╥ pinned search_path. Sums over **CURRENT** labor_logs (anti-join + tombstone filter, ADR 0009 Б─■ mirrors the cost engine) where `worker_type_snapshot='dc'` (own labor = payroll overhead, NOT transfer-priced Б├▓ excluded, as it's absent from the б╖2 formula), valued at the worker's per-level sell rate: `(fullБ├▓1, halfБ├▓0.5) ц≈ (internal_sell unless wp_economics.is_external Б├▓ external_sell)`; `coalesce(Б─╕,0)`. **is_external** = `coalesce((select is_external from wp_economics where wp=p_wp), false)` (no row = internal, U2 posture). **Ungraded DC Б├▓ 0** Б─■ the inner join to `sell_rate_table` drops a NULL-level worker, so an ungraded DC can never silently inflate profit; **decision: contribute 0, no side-effect flag** (pure read; surfacing the ungraded-DC-day count = U3b's profit struct). **Level = live grade** (labor_logs has no level snapshot; level-at-time = later refinement, noted). **Gate super_admin + project_director only** (no project_manager ref Б├▓ ADR 0058 pgTAP 90/91 untouched); **null-safe `is distinct from` form** denies NULL-role/service-role (rls-self-check-coalesce trap) Б├▓ 42501; unknown WP Б├▓ P0001 (typo errors, never a misleading 0). Reads zero-grant money tables (definer bypasses RLS); **invoked under the caller's authed session** (real super/director JWT so current_user_role() resolves), never the admin client Б─■ like freeze. Execute lockdown: `revoke all from public; grant execute to authenticated`. Pure read Б├▓ **no audit, no enum-add**. **pgTAP 101** (12 asserts: has_function+secdef; gate super+director pass / pmб╥site_adminб╥visitor 42501; internal WP senior-full 800 + mid-half 350 = **1150**; same crew external = **1375** and `>` internal; edge WP = **290** [only junior current-half counts: ungradedБ├▓0, own-with-level excluded, superseded-old excluded, tombstone excluded]; unknown WP P0001). Verify: lintб╥typecheckб╥test **188/1268**б╥db:pushб╥**db:test 101 files/1962/0** (was 1950 Б├▓ +12)б╥db:types (`wp_labor_sell` added) Б─■ all green. **Spec U3 detail authored first** (like U1/U2/U2b). **NEXT = U3b** full profit assembly (subtract equipment [spec 141/146] + materials [purchasing] from `wp_economics.budget`, **reconcile to GL** ADR 0057 Б─■ derive from, not a second costing path) Б├▓ U4 settlement ц≈ project multiplier Б├▓ U5 coin distribution Б├▓ U6 shop. **Open dial (flag, not blocking):** markup % still wants real **utilization data** for a solvent default Б─■ rates are editable/seeded, so the mechanism is built; operator should sanity-check sell rates vs actual billable-vs-idle DC-days before go-live.

## Spec 161 U2 - WP economic identity: budget + internal/external (ADR 0060) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-20.** Second economics unit. Migration `20260761000000_wp_economics.sql`. The WP's profit-engine inputs, isolated so **budget keeps the MONEY posture** (the profit denominator, hidden from non-HT DCs) instead of leaking through a `work_packages` column grant Б─■ mirrors `wp_labor_costs`. **`wp_economics`** (one row per WP, upserted): `work_package_id` PK+FK (on delete cascade), `budget numeric(20,4)` null (Б┴╔0 when set), `is_external boolean not null default false`, updated_by/at. **Zero authenticated grant** (RLS on, revoke all Б─■ pm/director/super read via admin client; SECURITY DEFINER setters are the only writers). **`set_wp_budget(wp,budget)`** = **project_director + super only** (the PD sets budget, ADR 0060 б╖1; anti-favoritism root = benchmark-to-scope) Б├▓ **no project_manager ref, so pgTAP 90/91 not triggered**; validates WP-exists + budgetБ┴╔0 (P0001); upserts budget preserving is_external; audits. **`set_wp_external(wp,bool)`** = **pm + director + super** (PM classifies; **references project_manager Б├▓ director included** per ADR 0058); upserts is_external preserving budget; audits. Both audit via generic `update` action (target wp_economics, target_id=wp), no enum-add. Gates **role-only** (not membership-scoped) for v1 Б─■ budget gate is see-all anyway; PM-membership on set_wp_external = later refinement. Nothing computes profit from these yet (U3). **pgTAP 99** (19 asserts: catalog table+PK+FK+cols; money posture no-auth-SELECT; set_wp_budget director+super set / pm+visitor 42501 / unknown-WP+negative P0001; set_wp_external pm sets / site_admin+visitor 42501 / unknown P0001; **upsert preserves the other column** Б─■ budget=120000 + is_external=true coexist; 3 sets audited). Verify: lintб╥typecheckб╥test **187/1264**б╥db:pushб╥**db:test 99 files/1936/0**б╥db:types Б─■ all green. **NEXT = U2b** (HT assignment: `projects.ht_worker_id`, one per project, PM-assigned) then **U3 WP profit engine** (reads sell_rate_table + wp_economics + labor + equipment Б├▓ profit; **needs operator UTILIZATION DATA for markup % calibration** Б─■ ADR 0060 open dial). **Lesson: money column on an existing table with a table-wide grant would leak Б─■ isolate WP money in a separate zero-grant table (wp_labor_costs pattern).**

## Spec 161 U1 - profit-sharing economics: per-level rate foundation (ADR 0060) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-20.** **ADR 0060 ACCEPTED this session** (was design-only) Б─■ operator approved the build with 3 anchors: **(a) editable dials seeded with defaults** (tune live, not hardcoded Б─■ satisfies "tune before build"); **(b) coin value = abstract points, per-item shop pricing, NO baht peg** (coins accrue as raw points; WP P&L + sell rates are baht, the separate reward layer settles from banked baht profit); **(c) narrow confiscation, vested coins are the worker's to keep** (resolves ADR 0060 б╖6 saver-bonus collision toward trust; ADR 0061 invariant). Spec 161 = the economics arc (U1 rate dials б╥ U2 WP profit center+budget+is_external+HT б╥ U3 WP profit engine б╥ U4 project settlementц≈multiplier б╥ U5 coin distributionБ├▓`coin_postings` б╥ U6 Nova shop+saver bonus+vesting). **U1 (THIS):** migration `20260760000000_sell_rate_foundation.sql`. `worker_level` **enum** (senior/mid/junior/apprentice; ADR 0060 б╖1); `workers.level` nullable col (category not money Б├▓ `grant select(level)` authenticated); **`sell_rate_table`** (level PK, baht `cost_band`/`internal_sell`/`external_sell` numeric(20,4), updated_by/at, nonneg check) Б─■ **MONEY posture: zero authenticated grant** (day_rate posture Б─■ operator reads via admin client behind requireRole super_admin), **SEEDED** 4 rows (senior 650/800/950 б╥ mid 550/700/850 б╥ junior 450/580/720 б╥ apprentice 380/480/600 Б─■ illustrative, operator retunes). **`set_worker_level(worker,level)`** SECURITY DEFINER super_admin (grading=operator economics, anti-favoritism б╖5; `is distinct from` null-safe gate; reuses `worker_change` audit kind=level_change). **`set_sell_rate(level,cost,internal,external)`** SECURITY DEFINER super_admin, nonneg (P0001), updates row + audits (action `update`, target sell_rate_table, payload old/new Б─■ generic action, no enum-add). **No `project_manager` ref Б├▓ pgTAP 90/91 not triggered.** Nothing READS the rates yet (U3). **pgTAP 98** (19 asserts: enum labels; workers.level col+type; table+PK; seed count=4 + senior value; money posture no-authenticated-SELECT; set_worker_level sets+audits+gate super/pm/visitor/unknown-worker; set_sell_rate updates+audits+gate+negative). ## Spec 160 - worker-ecosystem foundation Stage 0 (ADR 0061) (2026-06-20)

Status: **U1 + U2 + U3 SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-20. STAGE 0 COMPLETE** (person + ledger + portal-home; economics deferred). Under ADR 0061 Б─■ the foundation spine before any economics; also the long-promised `DC Б├▓ Project` correction (closes the original "site admins can't find the DCs" thread; DC belongs to a project, not a crew, per [[prc-ops-pay-model]]). Units: **U1 DC-as-person + project assignment** (add `workers.project_id` nullable FK + append-only `worker_project_moves` stream mirroring equipment_movements + `assign_worker_to_project` RPC pm/super + **drop the `workers_dc_has_contractor` force-tie** so a DC needs no contractor; additive/reversible; pgTAP 95) б╥ U2 event-sourced coin-ledger skeleton (append-only `coin_postings`, derived balance, pluggable sources Б─■ no economics) б╥ U3 portal as the worker's home (extend ADR 0051). **Build order (ADR 0061 decided): Stage 0 first; coin dials + economy deferred.**

**U1 detail (SHIPPED 2026-06-20):** migrations `20260756000000_worker_project_assignment.sql` (+ fix-forward `20260757000000_worker_assignment_director_gate.sql`). Adds `workers.project_id uuid null references projects(id)` (current assignment; granted to authenticated like the other non-rate columns; NO backfill Б─■ data-only follow-up); **DROPS** CHECK `workers_dc_has_contractor` (a DC may now have a null contractor; `contractor_id` column + `workers_own_has_no_contractor` kept); append-only `worker_project_moves` (`worker_id`/`project_id` nullable=unassigned/`moved_at`/`moved_by`/`reason`, RLS on, **zero write grant Б─■ RPC-only**, no update/delete, definer-owner insert bypasses); `assign_worker_to_project(p_worker,p_project,p_reason)` SECURITY DEFINER pinned search_path, gate **pm/super/director** Б├▓ else 42501, sets `project_id` + appends a move row + an `audit_log` row (reuses `worker_change` action, `payload.kind='project_move'`) in one tx; worker-not-found Б├▓ P0001. **No economics** (spine only). **pgTAP 95** (25 asserts: catalog col+FK; moves table append-only no UPDATE/DELETE/INSERT priv; CHECK dropped+kept; relaxed-CHECK lives_ok; RPC secdef; pm sets+appends+audits; sa/visitor 42501; super second-move historyБ├▓2). Verify: lintб╥typecheckб╥test **187 files/1258**б╥db:pushб╥**db:test 95 files/1860/0**б╥db:types Б─■ all green. **LESSONS:** (1) **project_director rides along** Б─■ ADR 0058 global invariants (pgTAP 90 "no PM-gated RPC without project_director" + 91 "no RLS policy names project_manager without project_director") broke because the spec's "pm/super" shorthand omitted director; every new PM gate/policy MUST add `project_director` Б─■ caught by db:test, fixed forward (20260757). (2) **Relaxing a CHECK breaks the test that pinned it** Б─■ pgTAP 29 asserted `throws_ok(dc-without-contractor, 23514)`; rewired to a catalog assertion that the CHECK is now dropped (no row added Б├▓ preserves the later `count(workers)=4`). (3) timestamp pick: latest applied migration was `20260755000000` (specs 155-157), not the `20260752000000` an audit-action grep surfaced Б─■ `migration list` before choosing.

**U2 detail (SHIPPED 2026-06-20):** migration `20260758000000_create_coin_ledger.sql`. Realizes ADR 0061 invariants 2+3 Б─■ the event-sourced coin-ledger spine, **NO economics** (sources named not valued; no value/earn-rules/settlement/shop/vesting/dials). `coin_source` **enum** (`profit_share`/`savers_bonus`/`behavior_bonus`; pluggable via future `add value`); append-only **`coin_postings`** (`worker_id` FK / `source` / `amount numeric(20,4)` **signed** Б─■ clawback = negative posting, not an edit / `reason` nonblankБ┴╓500 / `occurred_at` / `created_by` / `created_at`; checks amountБ┴═0 + reason; index worker+occurred_at). **Money/authority posture:** RLS on, `revoke all`, **zero write grant (RPC-only)**, SELECT policy **super_admin-only** (worker-sees-own waits for U3 portal); **self-auditing** like equipment_movements Б├▓ no audit_log row, no audit_action. **`coin_balance(worker) numeric`** = `coalesce(sum(amount),0)` Б─■ **SECURITY INVOKER** so it respects the read policy (non-operator sees 0, no leak); **balance always derived, never stored**. **`post_coins(worker,source,amount,reason,occurred_at)`** SECURITY DEFINER pinned search_path, gate **`current_user_role() is distinct from 'super_admin'`** (null-safe Б─■ the rls-self-check-coalesce trap; a single `<>` would open on NULL) Б├▓ 42501; validates worker-exists/amountБ┴═0/reason (P0001); inserts with `created_by=auth.uid()`. **No `project_manager` in any gate/policy Б├▓ ADR 0058 invariants (pgTAP 90/91) not triggered** (lesson applied from U1 Б─■ super_admin-only is intentional). **pgTAP 96** (28 asserts: catalog table+cols+FK+enum labels; append-only no U/D/INSERT priv; secdef + coin_balance exists; super postsБ├▓balance 100Б├▓150; negative clawback netsБ├▓120; ledger grew to 3; zero-amount/blank-reason/unknown-worker P0001; pm/sa/visitor 42501; super reads / non-operator reads 0 via RLS). Verify: lintб╥typecheckб╥test **187/1264**б╥db:pushб╥**db:test 96 files/1888/0**б╥db:types Б─■ all green.

**U3 detail (SHIPPED 2026-06-20):** migration `20260759000000_crew_assignments_portal.sql` (read-only RPC, no table/grant change). Realizes ADR 0061 invariant 5/6 (portal = worker's home) as the **first Stage-0 step**: the external DC portal (`/portal`, ADR 0051) crew list now shows **each member's current project** (U1 `workers.project_id`) Б─■ record, not coin. **`get_my_crew_assignments()`** SECURITY DEFINER, returns `(worker_id,name,active,project_id,project_code,project_name)` for the caller's OWN crew (`workers.contractor_id = current_user_contractor_id()`, ADR 0051 binding), left-joined to `projects` Б─■ the definer join lets an external contractor read **only their assigned projects' names** past the staff-scoped projects RLS; unbound/staff caller (NULL binding) Б├▓ zero rows; `revoke public/anon, grant execute authenticated` (get_my_dc_payments posture). **`loadPortalData` swaps the crew RLS query for the RPC** (fan size + concurrency unchanged); portal renders project under each crew name or "Ю╦╒Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╧└Ю╦║Ю╧┬Ю╧└Ю╦■Ю╧┴Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╚Ю╦≥Ю╦■Ю╧┌Ю╦└Ю╦ёЮ╦┤Ю╦│Ю╦╡Ю╦ё" (graceful pre-backfill, like the picker). **COINS DELIBERATELY EXCLUDED from the portal** Б─■ ADR 0060 б╖4 makes external DCs' coins **invisible** (unlock only on Internal invite) + ADR 0061 **gift-first** (first experience = record, not the opaque coin); `coin_postings` stays super_admin-only. **pgTAP 97** (10 asserts: secdef; contractor A sees only own crew + project code/name resolved; never B's crew; B sees own + null project when unassigned; unbound/staff Б├▓ 0 rows). **vitest** load-portal-data (crew fan member = RPC, assignment shape). Verify: lintб╥typecheckб╥test **187/1264**б╥db:pushб╥**db:test 97 files/1898/0**б╥db:types Б─■ all green. **Verified-by-checklist** (portal auth-gated Б├▓ preview /login on cloud PC; pgTAP carries RPC security; operator on-device = acceptance).

**STAGE 0 COMPLETE (U1+U2+U3).** **Open / next (own units):** **backfill existing DCs' `project_id`** (data-only Б─■ BLOCKED on operator's DCБ├▓project mapping; lights up both the spec 158 U2 picker's in-project section AND the U3 portal crew-project line). **Worker-sees-own-coins** on the portal Б─■ deferred to the Internal-invite / policy-evolution step (ADR 0060 б╖4 + invariant 6); not built. **Economics** (coin value/earn-rules/settlement/shop/vesting, ADR 0060 dials) Б─■ the next major arc, all deferred per ADR 0061 build order until the dials are tuned with the operator. Spec 158 U3 (SA-adds-DC-on-spot; operator sign-off first).

## Spec 159 U1 - subcontractor vs DC terminology consistency (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending full-suite green + commit). Operator: "DC setting is confusing Б─■ Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡/DC, Ю╦≈Ю╦╣Ю╦║Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥." Root cause: **"Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡" overloaded 3 ways** Б─■ (1) general WP contractor [LEAVE, operator], (2) subcontractor `category=contractor` [firm pays its own crew], (3) DC `category=dc` [PRC pays directly] mislabeled Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡ on several surfaces. **Taxonomy already exists** (`contractor_category` + `contractor_subtype` enums; Contacts tabs render DC Ю╦ Ю╦ёЮ╦╢Ю╦╘Ю╦╠Ю╦≈/Ю╦⌡Ю╦ёЮ╦╟Ю╦┬Ю╦Ё/Ю╦┼Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦└Ю╦ёЮ╦╡Ю╦╖) Б─■ NO schema change. **U1:** SSOT `SUBCONTRACTOR_LABEL = "Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡Ю╦┼Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦┤"` in labels.ts; rewired the 4 subcontractor surfaces to it (contacts-tabs TAB*LABEL.contractors + CONTRACTOR_FIELDS name + addLabel; contacts/crews title+h1; contacts/[type]/[id] TYPE_CONFIG label; settings crews door label+hint Б─■ kills the `Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡/DC` slash-merge Б├▓ `Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡Ю╦┼Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦┤ / DC`). DC tab/subtypes untouched (already consistent). **CAUGHT: "Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡" is a SUBSTRING of "Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡Ю╦┼Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦┤"** Б├▓ consistency guards assert presence-of-Ю╦┼Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦┤ / absence-of-exact-merged-string, never absence-of-Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡. **TDD:** source-guard `contact-subcontractor-label.test.ts` (SSOT value; 4 surfaces reference the constant; settings no longer has `Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡/DC`). First test wrongly asserted the literal Б─■ but SSOT means surfaces hold the \_constant name*, so the guard checks constant usage (the stronger anti-drift check).

**Open questions (OUT Б─■ own units):** **U2 DC-side de-Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡** Б─■ labor-cost-view (`dc: "Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡"`, `Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡ (DC)`), /payroll ("Ю╦└Ю╧┬Ю╦╡Ю╧│Ю╦ёЮ╦┤Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡"), the DC-worker **parent picker** (worker-roster-manager + workers/actions + group-workers UNKNOWN label), the DC **portal** ("Ю╦·Ю╦╜Ю╦ёЮ╧▄Ю╦≈Ю╦╠Ю╦╔Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡"), the role label `contractor: "Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡ (DC)"` all still call a DC "Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡"; needs the operator's chosen DC-crew word (e.g. Ю╦≈Ю╦╣Ю╦║ DC / Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦│Ю╦╠Ю╦■ DC) first. General-WP "Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡" stays generic (operator).

## Spec 158 U2 - project-scope the labor picker (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-20.** Verify: lint б╥ typecheck б╥ full test **187 files / 1264 / 0** green (**no DB change** Б─■ reads the spec 160 U1 `workers.project_id` column). Callers: PM WP page (via `loadWorkPackageDetail` Б─■ threads `wp.project_id`; `WorkPackageDetailData.labor` gains `projectWorkerIds`, fallback `[]`, concurrency-test mock updated) + SA review page (passes `wp.project_id`). **TDD:** `labor-group-workers.test.ts` (+3 partition cases) + `labor-log-zone.test.tsx` (+3: in-project ahead of others via `compareDocumentPosition`; no heading when empty; in-project tick submits). **Verified-by-checklist** (the WP page is auth-gated Б├▓ browser preview only renders /login on the cloud PC with no creds; the 6 component/pure tests carry the contract; operator on-device = acceptance). **Deferred (own units):** U3 SA-adds-DC-on-spot (role+RLS+create-RPC, must not expose `day_rate`; operator sign-off first); backfill existing DCs' `project_id` (data-only, spec 160 follow-up); destination = spec 130 DC self-report.

## Spec 158 U1 - DC labor picker search/filter (bridge) (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending commit). Verify: lint + typecheck + full test **186 files / 1252 / 0** green (no DB change). No schema / role / money change. **TDD:** extend `labor-group-workers.test.ts` (filterRoster cases) + `labor-log-zone.test.tsx` (search hides non-matches; pre-filter selection still submitted). **Deferred (own units):** U2 project-scope the picker (workers have no project link Б─■ scope by contractor / prior labor_logs / explicit link?); U3 SA-adds-DC-on-spot (role+RLS+create-RPC, must not expose `day_rate` money); destination = spec 130 self-report.

## Spec 157 - delete an empty work package (Tier 1) (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending suite green + commit). ADR 0059 б╖3. First delete path for WPs. `delete_work_package(p_work_package_id)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC: gate pm/super/**director** + `can_see_wp()`; **refuses (P0001) if ANY child exists** (photo_logs / labor_logs / approvals / purchase_requests / work_package_members / dependencies) else deletes; writes an audit_log row (event wp_deleted + code/name). Server action `delete-actions.ts` maps P0001 Б├▓ "cancel instead" message; `WpDeleteControl` (ConfirmDialog, no window.confirm) in the manager-only block, navigates to /projects/[id] on success (the WP is gone Б├▓ router.refresh would 404). **TDD:** pgTAP `94` (15 asserts: catalog, FK-blocks-delete, pm empty-delete+gone+audit, super+director see-all, photo/labor/PR Б├▓ P0001 + survives, sa-member+visitor role-deny, non-member pm membership-deny) + vitest `wp-delete-control` (confirmБ├▓deleteБ├▓navigate; historyБ├▓inline error+no-nav).

**KEY CORRECTION Б─■ the FK premise was wrong.** The investigation + ADR 0059 + spec 157 claimed `labor_logs.work_package_id` was a **bare column with no FK** (orphan risk) needing an "adjacent FK migration." **It already HAS an FK** (`references work_packages(id)`, NO ACTION Б├▓ blocks WP delete with 23503; migration 20260619000300 line 22). So spec 157 dropped the FK migration Б─■ **one migration only** (the RPC). ADR 0059 + spec 157 amended in place with correction notes. The empty-guard is still essential anyway: without it, deleting a WP would CASCADE-delete its purchase_requests / members / dependencies (silent data loss) and abort on the append-only photo_logs/approvals triggers. LESSON: verify FK existence by reading the table migration, not a summary Б─■ `references` on the column line is the FK.

**Verify:** db:push (prod) + db:test (file 94) + db:types + lint + typecheck + full test Б─■ green (below).

**Open questions (OUT):** **Tier 2 cancel/restore** for WPs WITH history (`cancelled` status enum value + exclusion from lenses/progress Б─■ own spec, own enum migration); cascade/bulk delete; un-delete (gone is gone Б─■ that's why Tier 2 exists). **ADR 0059 б╖Consequences "labor_logs FK debt" is now void** (FK exists).

## Spec 155 - bind a work package to a deliverable (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending full-suite green + commit). ADR 0059 б╖1. Closes the gap: `work_packages.deliverable_id` was settable ONLY by the manual seed script Б─■ no post-create write path, so in-app WPs were permanently ungrouped. Added `set_work_package_deliverable(p_work_package_id, p_deliverable_id)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC: gate pm/super/**project_director** + `can_see_wp()` membership (ADR 0056/0058, the reopen precedent); NULL = ungroup; a non-null deliverable must share the WP's project (cross-project/unknown Б├▓ 22023); no audit (benign metadata). Server action `deliverable-actions.ts` + a manager-only `WpDeliverableControl` native-select on the WP-detail page (Ю╦╒Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╧└Ю╦║Ю╧┬Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦│Ю╦╔Ю╦╦Ю╧┬Ю╦║ + each Ю╦┤Ю╦╖Ю╦■Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥); loader gained `deliverable_id`; the project's deliverables ride alongside the loader (planner-gated, no waterfall). **TDD:** pgTAP `92` (13 asserts: catalog, pm-member bind/clear, super + director see-all, cross-project/unknown 22023, sa-member + visitor role-deny 42501, non-member pm membership-deny 42501) + vitest `wp-deliverable-control.test.tsx` (renders ungrouped+each, binds chosen id, clears to null). **Verify:** db:push (prod) + db:test **92 files / 1809 / 0** + db:types + lint + typecheck green.

**Two deviations from the spec doc (both deliberate):** (1) unknown WP Б├▓ **42501** (membership gate runs first; can_see_wp is false for a missing WP Б─■ we don't disclose existence to non-members), NOT the doc's "false". (2) Took **two migrations** Б─■ `20260753000000` (RPC) then `20260753000100` (CREATE OR REPLACE adding `p_deliverable_id uuid default null`) Б─■ because supabase typegen marks a no-default arg as required non-null `string`, so the server action couldn't pass null; the default makes it optional Б├▓ the house omit-to-clear idiom (set_work_package_schedule). **Lesson: a nullable RPC arg the app must pass NULL/omit needs `default null` so typegen marks it optional Б─■ author it in the first migration.** Transient `cli_login_postgres` SASL circuit-breaker hit when db:push ran concurrent with db:test Б─■ retry alone clears it; don't run two supabase CLI ops at once.

**Open questions (OUT):** `create_deliverable` (in-app Ю╦┤Ю╦╖Ю╦■Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥ creation Б─■ until it ships, binding is inert on in-app-created projects); deliverable at CREATE time (extend create_work_package + add-WP-sheet picker); bulk re-bind/drag UI.

## Spec 154 - coordinator read-only project view (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE Б─■ shipped + pushed to prod (commit 609a0ab, origin/main 2026-06-19/20). Origin spec 143 / ADR 0056. `project_coordinator` is in PROJECT_VIEW_ROLES (reads /projects + /projects/[id]) but NOT SITE_STAFF_ROLES, so on /projects/[id] it falls through to the SA/PM main branch which links every WP row to the WP detail + renders a calendar chip Б─■ both gate `requireRole(SITE_STAFF_ROLES)`, deny coordinator Б├▓ redirect Б├▓ /projects (dead links / bounce). Fix = stop rendering links it can't follow, NOT widen any gate (ADR 0056 keeps WP detail + schedule SITE_STAFF-only). One predicate `canOpenWp = SITE_STAFF_ROLES.includes(ctx.role)`; WorklistRow + WorkPackageList gain optional `canOpen` (default true Б├▓ existing call sites unchanged); when false the row is a non-interactive container (no Link/href/hover/focus/chevron, list-enter animation kept). Calendar chip gated on canOpenWp. Coordinator keeps the manager-grade lens list, just non-clickable; NOT routed into the procurement branch. TDD: worklist-row.test.tsx (canOpen false Б├▓ no link, name/status still render; true/omitted Б├▓ one WP-detail link) + work-package-list.test.tsx (canOpen false Б├▓ zero row links; default Б├▓ links).

**Open questions (OUT of scope, not built):** (1) Fix B = coordinator read-only WP DETAIL + schedule Б─■ contradicts ADR 0056, needs an ADR amendment first. (2) WP-detail/schedule requireRole gates stay coordinator-excluded (correct). (3) Read-only row styling beyond removing tap affordance.

## Spec 151 U1 - lazy client bundles: defer offline-queue runner (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE (U1), build-verified; **first-load delta NOT numerically verifiable in this env** (see caveat). Bundle investigation: total client JS ~542kb gz; the 125kb gz chunk = supabase-js (browser client) + zod. zod is imported ONLY by `env.ts`/`env.server.ts` (env validation at import); the browser client by 9 client components Б─■ 8 route-scoped/tap-gated, but **`UploadQueueRunner` is mounted in the root `layout.tsx`**, so it drags that 125kb chunk onto EVERY page's first paint. Fix: `src/components/features/photos/upload-queue-runner-lazy.tsx` Б─■ a `'use client'` wrapper that `next/dynamic`-imports the runner with `ssr:false`; layout renders the wrapper. Safe: the runner is a background drainer for LEFTOVER offline uploads (renders null unless queued; replay idempotent ADR 0039; in-page phase-uploader unaffected), so loading it a beat after hydration is harmless. Verification: lint + typecheck + `pnpm build` all green (exit 0). **CAVEAT Б─■ couldn't prove the win numerically:** Turbopack's prod build emits no per-route First Load JS table, and there's no runnable app here (no auth/prod URL), so the ~110kb first-paint reduction (124kb deferred Б┬▓ ~14kb split overhead; total bundle ticked 542Б├▓556kb because the chunk still EXISTS, just lazy) rests on the `dynamic(ssr:false)` framework guarantee, not a measurement. **Confirm on laptop:** preview + Network tab (the supabase chunk should load AFTER first paint, not block it), or add `@next/bundle-analyzer`. **Next (later, all need a runnable app to verify):** dynamic-import the 8 tap-gated uploader/sheet components per-route; Tier-2 in-page Suspense; middleware getUser; infra.

## Spec 152 U3 - project_director role: table write RLS (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE (U3) Б─■ **FEATURE COMPLETE**. Final unit: adds `project_director` to every RLS policy whose role list literally names `project_manager`. **Why it matters:** some core PM actions are direct-table writes gated by RLS, NOT RPCs Б─■ most importantly **approving a work package** (an INSERT into `approvals`), so without U3 a director could not approve. Also covers deliverables/reports/work*packages/photo_logs/photo_markups/purchase_requests writes, project_members/work_package_members manage, and the master-table READS (clients/contractors/suppliers/service_providers/equipment\*/workers) that list PM directly. **Method: reconstructed the 48 policies from the LIVE catalog (`pg_policies`), appended `'project_director'::user_role` to each role `ARRAY[...]` (Postgres reverse-compiles `in()` Б├▓ `= ANY(ARRAY[])`, and has no CREATE OR REPLACE POLICY, so DROP+CREATE).** Migration `20260752000000_project_director_write_rls.sql` Б─■ **48 policies / 58 role lists** widened (UPDATE policies carry PM in both USING + WITH CHECK). **NOT touched:** project-scoped SELECTs (gate on `can_see*\*`Б├▓ see-all for director since U1, never name PM literally); every super_admin-alone operator policy (no PM literal Б├▓ no match). **Test (REDБ├▓GREEN):** pgTAP`91`Б─■ completeness catalog (per-field: no policy names PM without director; 48 before Б├▓ 0 after), behavioural lives_ok (director inserts an approval + updates a work_package directly on an UNINVOLVED WP Б─■ see-all + role), negative control (visitor still denied Б├▓ 42501). No TS change. db:push applied to prod; db:test 91 files / 0 fail. **project_director is now a complete see-all project_manager: sees everything, every RPC action, every direct-table write.** Built in isolated worktree off`main`@#77.

## Incident: AppSheet EMAXCONNSESSION (2026-06-11)

Operator screenshot: AppSheet app failed to load Б─■ 'max clients reached in session mode, pool_size: 48' on projects + users reads. Diagnosis: AppSheet data source pointed at the SESSION pooler (5432, per go-live checklist Step 2 wording); Supavisor session pools are per-DB-user with a 48-client cap, and AppSheet's parallel sync burst exhausted appsheet_writer's pool. pg_stat_activity showed ZERO held appsheet_writer backends at diagnosis time Б─■ burst, not a leak; nothing to terminate; no prod change made. Fix: operator repoints AppSheet to the TRANSACTION pooler (6543). Checklist Step 2 now documents the port split (5432 = smoke ritual only). Raising session pool_size is not viable (already near the compute tier's max_connections). Open question: if AppSheet misbehaves on transaction mode (prepared-statement quirks), revisit Б─■ fallback is a dedicated session pool budget discussion.

## Unit: architecture revision doc Б─■ entrepreneur lens (2026-06-11)

- **Status:** COMPLETE (doc-only, advisory). Operator brief: "revise the architecture of this app; think like an entrepreneur, not just technical."
- **Deliverable:** [`docs/architecture-revision-2026-06.md`](./architecture-revision-2026-06.md) Б─■ strategic assessment of the whole system by business criteria (cost/month, ops burden per change, engagement, sellability, moat).

### Key positions taken (all pending operator sign-off Б─■ б╖6 of the doc)

1. **AppSheet = rented ground.** Stop investing: cancel the unwritten ADR 0029 image bridge, build the in-app procurement surface + suppliers table instead (derive triggers are already writer-agnostic per ADR 0025; `procurement` role waits in the enum), demote AppSheet to read-only, then retire. Kills the per-schema-change operator tax, the Tier-2 write smoke, the EMAXCONNSESSION incident class, and the licence line.
2. **LINE notification outbox promoted to next feature slot** Б─■ audit triggers already detect every hand-off event; they just don't deliver. Outbox table + drainer + LINE Messaging API channel.
3. **Railway retired when touched** Б─■ PDF on-demand (route handler spike first) or Edge Function; end-state two platforms.
4. **Tenancy decided on purpose:** instance-per-customer for now + tenant-clean discipline + spin-up runbook; multi-tenant schema deferred until customer #2 is real.
5. Migration rehearsal stage (preview branch/scratch project) before destructive pushes; photo client-side downscale question raised; crew capability-URL uploads parked as v2 differentiator; dormant owner_id/work_package_members cleanup listed.

### Open questions

- The four б╖6 operator decisions (AppSheet sunset, notifications next, tenancy posture, photo downscale).
- No code/schema/test change this unit; suites untouched (555 pgTAP / 283 unit as of a42f083).

### Spec 32 adversarial verification (3-lens workflow) Б─■ fixes landed pre-commit

- **Blast-radius + discipline lens Б─■ MAJOR, fixed:** `.env.example` shipped the two optional vars as empty assignments; dotenv loads `VAR=` as "" and `.optional()` rejects "" Б├▓ every fresh "copy .env.example" local boot (and a blank Vercel value) would crash env validation at import time. Fixed both ends: `optionalNonEmpty` preprocess (emptyБ├▓absent) in env.server.ts + lines commented out in .env.example + 3 new env.test.ts cases (the existing per-var missing/empty pattern now covers the new vars).
- **Blast-radius minors, fixed:** photo_logs uploader enrichment included tombstone rows (uploaded_by = REMOVER per ADR 0015) Б├▓ `.not("storage_path","is",null)`; no maxDuration on a 50ц≈N-push route Б├▓ `export const maxDuration = 60`; PostgREST 1000-row cap on the uploader query Б├▓ loud warn when hit (pilot volumes far below).
- **Security minors, fixed:** drain secret now compared via sha256+timingSafeEqual; LINE 5000-char text limit enforced by truncation in pushLineMessage (an oversized user comment was a deterministic 400 Б├▓ burned all 3 attempts Б├▓ actor-controlled notification suppression) + unit test; pgTAP file 25 hardened +11 asserts (plan 37): authenticated UPDATE/DELETE denial, anon denial, policies_are ZERO, EXECUTE denial on invoke_notification_drain for anon+authenticated (PostgREST RPC exposure pin), all four capture functions SECURITY DEFINER + pinned search_path, pr_created WHEN-guard negative, and the headline failure-swallowing posture PROVEN (outbox renamed away inside the transaction Б├▓ WP write still lands, zero rows captured).
- **Discipline:** payload.ts (5th pure module) had no tests Б├▓ notification-payload.test.ts added (key mapping, type-narrowing drops, malformed input); recorded here as declared addition alongside the admin.ts typing pull-in. pr_cancelled trigger breadth (anyБ├▓cancelled vs spec's approvedБ├▓cancelled) recorded in ADR 0037 as deliberate, with the audit-widening caveat for any future self-cancel unit.

Final suite state: 318 unit / 592 pgTAP / 27 e2e, typecheck+lint clean, drain endpoint live-probed 503 not_configured pre-activation.

## Spec 34 - client photo downscale (2026-06-11)

Status: COMPLETE (operator phone pass = acceptance, spec б╖3). Implements ADR 0036: the downscaled file IS the original; max 2000px long edge, JPEG 0.8; downscale is an optimization NEVER a gate Б─■ every failure path (HEIC on non-Safari, decode/encode errors, toBlob null) uploads the original unchanged; small files pass through with EXIF intact (orientation correct either way: re-encode bakes orientation via createImageBitmap imageOrientation:'from-image', passthrough keeps EXIF).

Built: src/lib/photos/downscale.ts (computeDownscaleTarget PURE + preparePhotoForUpload browser seam) + photoExtToMime in path.ts Б─■ RED confirmed pre-impl, 11 unit tests. Integrated in ALL THREE uploaders at the ext-derivation point (ext flips to jpeg on re-encode BEFORE path building): phase-uploader (PendingUpload now stores prepared blob + lastModifiedMs scalar Б─■ no raw File in state; retries reuse prepared bytes), attachment stager, delivery uploader. No DB/storage diff.

### Adversarial verification (2-lens) Б─■ fixes landed pre-commit

- Transparent PNG/WebP over the cap re-encoded onto a BLACK background (canvas default substrate under toBlob jpeg) Б├▓ white fill before drawImage.
- REAL race (stager deferred mode): awaiting prepare BEFORE staging the chip meant a create-form submit during a slow phone decode flushed without the in-flight photo Б─■ orphaned 'staged' chip, and a SECOND submission would have attached it to the WRONG purchase request. Fix: chips stage synchronously as 'preparing' (new status + Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╧─Ю╦∙Ю╦ёЮ╦╣Ю╦╒Ю╦║Ю╦ёЮ╦╧Ю╦⌡Б─╕ display), prepare jobs tracked in a ref, flush() awaits outstanding prepares THEN reads a fresh items ref (the closure's items is stale after an await Б─■ itemsRef pattern).
- createImageBitmap orientation made explicit (imageOrientation:'from-image' Б─■ old Firefox/WebViews don't default to it); ext! assertions narrowed; stager header comment de-drifted; rounding test now exercises a genuinely fractional edge (3000ц≈1000 Б├▓ 667).

Suite: 336 unit / 27 e2e green; pgTAP untouched (627). OPERATOR (acceptance): fresh camera photo on a test-safe WP Б├▓ renders correctly oriented; Storage object ~hundreds of KB not MB (dashboard read-only check). Open seams: Web Worker offload (with the offline-queue spec), HEIC polyfill, quality/size UI, retroactive processing (never Б─■ append-only).

## Spec 35 - offline-tolerant upload queue, WP phase photos (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator phone pass = acceptance: airplane mode -> photo -> banner -> close browser -> signal -> reopen -> photo lands). ADR 0039. A selected phase photo is never lost: persisted to IndexedDB at selection (survives crash/close/navigation, iOS + Android Б─■ NO Background Sync dependency), uploads live exactly as before on good signal, global UploadQueueRunner (root layout; banner Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦ёЮ╦╧Ю╦⌡ N Ю╦ёЮ╦╧Ю╦⌡ only when items wait) drains leftovers on mount/online/visibility/event/backoff (5sб╥2^n cap 5min).

Architecture: replay is IDEMPOTENT end-to-end so live-path/runner/multi-tab overlap is harmless BY DESIGN Б─■ bytes 409 Б┤▓ alreadyExists Б┤▓ advance; addPhoto gains a 23505 replay path. Pure core (processQueue/QueueStore/classify/backoff) test-first vs in-memory store Б─■ 15 unit tests; IDB store + runner are browser seams (house posture). Items NEVER auto-dropped (evidence); attempts only widen backoff.

### Adversarial verification (2-lens, verdict FAIL -> all fixed pre-commit)

- MAJOR (security): the 23505 verify originally checked id-exists only Б─■ photo ids are readable role-wide, so a forged replay with a foreign photo id (e.g. a before-photo id + phase='after') would return ok AND flip the WP to pending_approval with zero after photos. Verify now requires the FULL replayed identity (id + work_package_id + phase + canonical storage_path).
- MAJOR (shared device): queue items now carry userId; the runner SKIPS foreign/ownerless items (uploaded_by is append-only Б─■ misattribution is uncorrectable). Post-logout blob persistence recorded in ADR 0039 as an accepted tradeoff; discard UI = seam.
- MAJOR (live-path resilience): addPhoto invocation throw (the exact flaky-signal case) stuck the tile and ABORTED the multi-file loop (remaining files never queued Б─■ silent loss) -> try/catch in insertOne + per-iteration isolation in handleFiles. Queue I/O (quota/private-mode IDB) wrapped non-fatal Б─■ the safety net can't break the live pipeline.
- MAJOR (idempotency gap): live uploadOne wasn't 409-tolerant Б─■ a runner/live overlap left a permanently-failing retry tile; now classifies alreadyExists and proceeds.
- Minors: banner staleness (notify after live remove; lock-unavailable branch refreshes count + short retry), pass-failure now reschedules (30s) instead of freezing, dead nowMs dep removed, projectId dropped from the persisted item (fileName kept for the discard seam, recorded), header lifecycle comment updated.

Suites: 349 unit / 27 e2e green; pgTAP untouched (627); no DB schema diff (addPhoto change is app-layer only). Open seams: reference/delivery photo queueing, manual discard UI, SW Background Sync, Web Worker downscale. OPERATOR: phone acceptance pass for specs 34+35 together (one outdoor session covers both).

## Spec 37 - offline queue for all photo kinds + manual discard (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator phone pass = acceptance, spec б╖2). Closes both ADR 0039 seams: the loss-proof queue now covers reference attachments and delivery-confirmation photos (not just WP phase photos), and the Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦ёЮ╦╧Ю╦⌡ banner expands into a per-item list with confirm-guarded Ю╦╔Ю╦  Б─■ the ONLY way an item leaves the queue without landing.

Legacy spec-35 items normalize to phase_photo on read (IDB schemaless Б─■ no version bump). Test-first: 5 new core tests (mixed-kind dispatch, normalization, bucket map, discard race).

### Adversarial verification (2-lens, FAIL -> all fixed pre-commit)

- MAJOR: addPurchaseRequestAttachment's status gate ran before the 23505 verify, so a replay whose insert LANDED but whose response was lost could never confirm after the PM decided Б─■ the queue item retried forever for a photo that was already live. Fixed: decided-parent path runs the identity-complete existence check first (read-only); never-landed items on decided parents are refusable BY DESIGN Б─■ the reference window closes at decision time (recorded in spec + ADR; discard is the designed out).
- Discard raced an in-flight pass: processQueue's put-backs could resurrect (or send) a just-discarded item. Fixed: QueueStore.has() re-checks before every put-back (pinned by unit test); confirm copy now promises only un-sent deletion.
- Shared-device hole in the NEW surface: the discard list let any device holder (incl. logged-out on /login) see and delete other users' un-sent evidence Б─■ contradicting the ADR 0039 skip-foreign stance. Fixed: foreign items render read-only without fileName (Ю╦ёЮ╦╧Ю╦⌡Ю╦┌Ю╦╜Ю╦┤Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╧┐Ю╦┼Ю╧┴Ю╦╜Ю╦╥Ю╧┬Ю╦≥ Б─■ Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╧─Ю╦┬Ю╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦┌Ю╦╜Ю╦┤Ю╧─Ю╦┌Ю╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦╙Ю╦╧Ю╧┬Ю╦ёЮ╦╟Ю╦ Ю╦ ).
- Deferred-mode queueing was dead code (userId never threaded to the create form) Б─■ silent loss on flush-with-bad-signal survived. Fixed: userId through PurchaseRequestForm at /requests + WP page.
- Delivery failure copy said "Ю╦╔Ю╦╜Ю╦┤Ю╧┐Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╧┬" which would make users re-pick under a NEW uuid Б├▓ duplicate rows when both landed. Copy now says queued-will-auto-send. a11y: role=status moved off the details element onto the count span (live region must not swallow disclosure semantics/buttons); summary marker restored.

Suites: 359 unit / 27 e2e green; pgTAP untouched (627); no schema diff. OPERATOR: the specs 34+35 phone pass extends to 37 (airplane-mode delivery photo -> banner -> reopen -> lands + auto-completes delivery per ADR 0030). ## Spec 42 - PWA standalone LINE re-login, iOS (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone pass = acceptance). Operator report: installed PWA loses login after logout; LINE re-login bounces through the LINE app to the system browser, session lands in the wrong cookie jar (iOS standalone jar is separate; CSRF state cookie also splits, so the browser-side callback dies oauth_failed). Fix per spec 42: disable_auto_login=true on the authorize URL for iOS standalone launches (verified against LINE Login v2.1 docs Б─■ keeps the whole flow in the PWA's in-app overlay via LINE web login), CSS-toggled standalone login anchor (?standalone=1, display-mode arbitrary variants, no 'use client' Б─■ ADR 0012 plain-anchor shape preserved), header logout CSS-hidden in standalone (profile-page logout stays, reachable via bottom tab). Android untested Б─■ flag is iOS-UA-gated to avoid regressing the shared-jar WebAPK flow.

Test-first: 3 new route tests (tests/unit/line-start-route.test.ts Б─■ env.server mocked at module level since serverEnv validates at import), 2 LoginButton tests, 1 AppHeader logout-wrapper pin. Playwright note: role-based locators ignore the display-hidden second anchor (a11y tree), so the existing e2e href pin survives untouched Б─■ 8/8 auth e2e green on chromium. Suites: 368 unit / lint / typecheck green; no DB diff.

Recorded limitation + seam: LINE accounts with no registered email/password cannot complete the web login form (mitigation: browser login -> reinstall PWA; site data copies into the container at install). Real fix if it bites = one-time handoff code minting the session in the PWA via the existing generateLink/verifyOtp machinery (spec 42 out-of-scope section). Supabase inactivity timeout must stay "never" (operator check, no code). OPERATOR: iPhone acceptance pass Б─■ install PWA, logout, log back in via LINE web login without leaving the app.

## Spec 43 - device-code handoff login for the installed PWA (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone pass = acceptance). Shipped 398f8da + types reconcile 1fd8df2 (typegen also caught up reap_stale_reports from spec 39); migration 20260618000100 applied via db push (dry-run showed zero drift first); pgTAP 656/656 (640 + file 28's 16). Operator hit spec 42's recorded limitation within minutes (LINE web login = QR or email/password; both unusable). ADR 0041: device-code handoff. PWA login tap -> POST /auth/handoff/start issues {state, device_code} row (login_handoffs, 10-min TTL, outbox zero-access posture) -> LINE auth with auto-login RESTORED (one-tap in LINE app) -> callback validates state against the DB row instead of the cookie (resolveCallbackFlow precedence: valid cookie always wins = browser path byte-equivalent), binds user_email + claims stash, status approved, shows return-to-app notice -> PWA polls /auth/handoff/poll, which atomically claims (approved->consumed) and mints the session onto the poll response via the ADR 0012 generateLink/verifyOtp pair - sb-\* cookies land in the PWA's own jar. Profile write parity (NULL-only + avatar refresh) runs at poll time from the stashed claims. Spec 42 items 1-2 reverted (disable_auto_login + ?standalone=1 anchor dead); logout hiding stands.

New surfaces: migration 20260618000100 + pgTAP file 28 (16 asserts), src/lib/auth/{line-authorize-url,line-token-exchange,handoff-flow}.ts (exchange/verify extracted - both callback paths verify identically), /auth/handoff/{start,poll} routes, StandaloneLoginButton ('use client' justified: fetch + window.open + poll orchestration; useSyncExternalStore for sessionStorage resume - react-hooks/set-state-in-effect rejects the mount-setState pattern, lesson banked), login page handoff=approved notice, proxy PUBLIC_PATHS +2. database.types.ts hand-extended pre-push; reconcile with pnpm db:types post-push. Suites: 395 unit / auth e2e 8/8 / prod build green / pgTAP 656. Security notes recorded in ADR 0041: device_code never in URLs, single-use via atomic claim, claim-before-mint burn tradeoff, uniform expired answers, device-grant phishing class accepted for internal user base (confirm-tap = hardening seam). Seams: poll rate limiting, Android pass.

## Spec 44 - handoff resume hardening, iOS process death (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone re-test = acceptance). First spec-43 field test failed: row reached approved (browser success page shown) but PWA never claimed - iOS killed the backgrounded PWA during the LINE/Safari excursion and sessionStorage died with it (no resume, no poll, idle button). Client-only fix in StandaloneLoginButton: (1) localStorage + expiry stamp (line_handoff_device_code / line_handoff_expires_at, 600s = server TTL; stale stamp reads as nothing-stored in the useSyncExternalStore snapshot, clearing only in handlers - no side effects in render), (2) popup opened SYNCHRONOUSLY in the tap gesture (window.open after await can fall outside iOS transient user activation), opener nulled, navigated after the start POST; blocked popup -> same-window fallback (safe now that the code persists), start failure closes the orphan popup. Server untouched - approved rows wait the full TTL for a late claimer by design. 8 component tests (popup contract, resume, stale-stamp idle, fallback). Suites: 398 unit / auth e2e 8/8. Lesson banked: iOS standalone PWA storage assumptions - sessionStorage NEVER survives the app-switch kill; any cross-app handshake state must live in localStorage with its own TTL.

## Spec 45 - handoff opens LINE in same window, no popup (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone re-test = acceptance). Spec-44 field test: home app went ALL WHITE on tap - iOS standalone PWAs have NO tab model; the spec-44 synchronous window.open('', '\_blank') swaps the visible view to a dead about:blank and the later popup navigation never reaches the user. Fix (client-only, third round on ADR 0041): popup path deleted; tap -> start POST -> store code (spec-44 localStorage+expiry) -> SAME-WINDOW navigation to LINE (no transient-activation concern). Return trip = spec 44's resume: PWA resumes (user closes out-of-scope top-bar view) or relaunches cold at start_url; any LoginButton page resumes the poll. Cancel pin caught a REAL bug: cancel from a resumed waiting state mutated only storage (no React state delta) so useSyncExternalStore never re-read - storage mutations now emit to subscribers (proper external store, not the noop-subscribe shortcut). Suites: 397 unit / auth e2e 8/8. Lessons banked: (1) standalone PWA = never window.open, same-window nav + persistent resume state is the pattern; (2) noop-subscribe useSyncExternalStore is a trap whenever mutations can happen without an accompanying state change.

Same-date-supersede assumption recorded (corrections/tombstones preserve work_date; a date-moving correction across the period boundary is a seam). Server: src/lib/labor/fetch-payroll.ts (server-only shared read backing BOTH surfaces so CSV and on-screen can't diverge; fetches all worker types in the window + resolves contractor names from contractors, CURRENT name not snapshotted - name-snapshot is a seam). UI: /pm/payroll Server Component (period = zero-client-JS GET form defaulting to the current Bangkok month; per-contractor cards with worker rows + subtotal + grand total; Ю╦■Ю╦╡Ю╦╖Ю╦≥Ю╧▄Ю╧┌Ю╦╚Ю╦╔Ю╦■ CSV is a plain <a download> NOT next/link so a prefetch can't fire the export) + /pm/payroll/export route handler (requireRole FIRST, text/csv attachment, no-store) + loading.tsx. PM_HUB_NAV +1 item Ю╦└Ю╧┬Ю╦╡Ю╦┬Ю╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦┤ -> /pm/payroll (4th; PM surfaces are already PM/super-gated so it leaks nothing to SA; hub-nav.test pin + comment updated). BottomTabBar is independently hardcoded (untouched) - a mobile payroll tab is a seam (payroll = back-office, PC-leaning). No pgTAP: no new DB object/RLS/grant - the existing grant tests already prove authenticated cannot read day_rate_snapshot, and the new reads go through the same trusted admin-client + requireRole(PM_ROLES) gate spec 68's cost view uses. Browser preview not feasible (LINE-OAuth wall + money-data seeding) - operator acceptance, same model as spec 68. Suites: 596 unit (+16 payroll, hub-nav pin updated) / lint / typecheck / prod build green. No DB diff. Seams: audit each export (action='export'), own-crew payroll, contractor-name snapshot, date-moving corrections, a "mark period paid" state, a mobile bottom-tab entry.

## Spec 71 - notes as backup capture: work-package notes (2026-06-13)

Status: COMPLETE (migration APPLIED to prod, pgTAP 801/801). (2) statuses as icons vs text -> DECISION: KEEP TEXT-ONLY (operator agreed) - color already carries the fast scan (spec 67 token canon), 13 statuses have no intuitive glyph, Thai-first + a11y want text; NO icon work. DESIGN call for notes: per-entity EDITABLE notes column (matches the existing purchase_requests.notes spec-48 + work_packages.description precedent + the operator's "notes field" mental model), NOT a generic polymorphic notes table (CLAUDE.md forbids mixed-content reference columns; a thread over-architects "a backup field"). Coverage audit found the gaps: editable WP remark, supplier/contractor notes, labor-day note. SCOPED v1 to the highest-value + cleanest slice -> WORK-PACKAGE notes (WP-centric principle #1); suppliers/contractors have NO edit UI today (created/selected only) and labor_logs is append-only, so those slices need their own surfaces/handling = recorded seams.

MODEL: work_packages.notes text null + CHECK (notes is null or length<=2000) [abuse backstop; app caps at 1000 = spec-48 cap; starts closing the queued DB-CHECK gap]. Write path = set_work_package_notes(p_work_package_id, p_notes) SECURITY DEFINER RPC MIRRORING set_work_package_contractor (spec 31): role gate site_admin/pm/super else 42501, search_path pinned, revoke-then-grant execute, nullif(btrim(p_notes),'') so blank clears to null, return found. WHY an RPC: SA is the on-site note author but work_packages UPDATE RLS is pm/super only - the RPC writes the notes column ONLY without handing SA every WP column (the spec-31 lesson). NO audit row (consistent with set_work_package_contractor - WP-column edits aren't individually audited; a note is benign ops text).

APP: validateWorkPackageNotes pure helper (trim, empty->null, 1000 cap) TDD-first; setWorkPackageNotes server action (UUID + cap validate, action gate, RPC relay, revalidatePath); WorkPackageNotes client component (controlled textarea + dirty/save/error/saved state, mirrors wp-assignment-panel) in the WP detail Ю╦┌Ю╧┴Ю╦╜Ю╦║Ю╦╧Ю╦╔Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥ zone (sa/pm/super reach it). typecheck caught the one trap: typegen types p_notes as a NON-NULL string, so the action passes validated.value ?? "" (the RPC's nullif maps "" -> null) rather than string|null. database.types.ts hand-extended then db:types regen reconciled EXACTLY (only delta vs HEAD = the notes column on Row/Insert/Update + the set_work_package_notes fn, p_notes: string - schema understanding confirmed).

TESTS: 8 unit (validate-notes x4 + work-package-notes component x4) RED then GREEN. pgTAP +11 in file 08: 3 catalog (notes text/nullable + has_function) + 8 behavioral (SA writes via RPC returns true + note landed, visitor 42501, procurement 42501 [reads WPs per spec 70 but never writes], unknown WP -> false, blank -> null x2, length CHECK rejects >2000 = 23514). Suites: 607 unit / 801 pgTAP / lint / typecheck / prod build all green.

SEAMS (the rest of "everywhere", each its own slice): supplier notes + contractor notes (need an edit surface first - none exists), labor-day note (labor_logs.note via a log_labor_day param, append-only carries through corrections), editable purchase-request note (purchase_requests.notes is write-once spec-48; making it editable is a posture change), PM-review-page (/pm/work-packages/[id]) read-only display of the WP note. SHIPPED: use-toast.ts (useToast hook + context + NO-OP fallback outside a provider so consumers degrade safely, never throw) + toast-provider.tsx (mounted in root layout WRAPPING {children} so a toast fired just before router.refresh survives the RSC re-render) + globals.css @keyframes toast-in gated by prefers-reduced-motion:no-preference (opt-in; reduced-motion=instant) + classes.ts TOAST_SUCCESS(emerald)/TOAST_ERROR (pinned). z-[45] fixed bottom above the 64px tab bar + safe-area. ## Spec 77 - app-feel slice 2: press/active tactile feedback (2026-06-13)

Status: COMPLETE (no DB; acceptance = operator eyeball). Second app-feel slice. Native apps respond on touch; only buttons had a press state (active:translate-y-px) - the cards/rows/tabs/chips/icons people tap had none, and iOS painted its grey tap-flash over them. Verified fact: navigator.vibrate is a no-op on iOS PWA, so :active states are the only "haptic" the primary users get. METHOD: an exhaustive Explore tap-target audit (22 targets lacking press feedback, grouped + traffic-ranked) -> press states on the high-traffic set. SHIPPED: (1) GLOBAL globals.css - -webkit-tap-highlight-color:transparent on html (kills the grey iOS flash) + touch-action:manipulation on a/button/summary/label/[role=button] (drops the ~300ms double-tap-zoom delay -> instant taps); biggest single win, covers every control. (2) active:bg-zinc-100 press tint on PR cards, WP list rows (flat+contained), project rows (sa+pm), PM queue rows; active:bg-slate-200 on the deliverable group toggle. (3) active:translate-y-px on ICON_CHIP/\_MUTED (back/gear/reports) + RefreshButton + RadioChip + the requests filter chips. (4) active:scale-95 on bottom-tab-bar items (transform, no reflow). ICON_CHIP was NOT byte-pinned (audit was wrong) so no pin churn. design-doctrine stays green (zinc/slate press hues, 44px floor kept). 634 unit / lint / typecheck / build green. DEFERRED (low-traffic, covered by the global): text <summary> toggles, desktop HubNav/AppHeader links, report download button, requests back link. NEXT app-feel slices: 3 optimistic UI (kill the 37 router.refresh flickers, careful per-surface), 4 bottom sheets, 5 motion (CSS @starting-style list-enter; route VT guarded spike).
