## Data-architecture hardening pass (2026-06-13) Б─■ audit ranks 1-9 shipped

Status: COMPLETE (all applied to prod under full operator autonomy; verify = operator can't see it, it's infra). Followed a 4-dimension multi-agent audit (normalization/scale/RLS-tenancy/AI-readiness) + synthesis. Full review + deferred roadmap persisted at docs/data-architecture-review-2026-06.md. Nine ranks, 8 migrations (20260625000100-000800) + 1 app change + 7 new pgTAP files (35-41); suite 865 assertions / 0 failures; typecheck/unit/build green. Shipped: (1+2) hot-path indexes - labor_logs superseded_by partial (anti-join) + work_date (the spec-69 payroll date-window was seq-scanning since both composites lead with worker/wp), purchase_requests(requested_by,supplier_id), work_packages(status,updated_at)+(contractor_id), workers(contractor_id,user_id). (5) revoke PUBLIC/anon EXECUTE on the 5 worker/labor mutation RPCs (the 0624 note-param DROP+CREATEs had reset grants to the PUBLIC default; internal current_user_role() gate was the only defense). (4) prune_notification_outbox daily cron (terminal rows >30d - the only disposable log table; audit_log/photo_logs/labor_logs are evidence, partition later). (6) COMMENT ON all 20 tables + load-bearing columns - was 0 table/4 column comments; makes the schema legible to text-to-SQL/AI. (7) purchase_requests.received_by_id FK (the one genuine free-text-where-FK-belongs column; populated on both write paths - record_site_purchase=auth.uid(), delivery trigger=uploader) + reports.params object CHECK + workers.contractor_id delete-block comment. (3) RLS EVAL-ONCE - the headline: every policy called auth.uid()/current_user_role() BARE, evaluated per-row (EXPLAIN-verified: "Filter: current_user_role()=ANY"). Wrapped in scalar subselects -> InitPlan, once per query (EXPLAIN-verified after). Transformed in-DB from pg_get_expr text (no hand-reproduction). 66/67 policies; photo_markups EXCLUDED - its INSERT policy has an inline self-referential subquery (tombstone-target), wrapping calls in either of its policies makes the self-reference re-apply a wrapped policy -> 42P17 recursion (cure = a SECURITY DEFINER tombstone helper like attachments use; deferred). Three migrations (000600 cursor-skip wrapped 34 + broke markups; 000700 snapshot-then-alter wrapped remaining 32 + began markup revert; 000800 finished markup revert). LESSONS: (a) a plpgsql FOR-IN-SELECT cursor over pg_policies skips rows when you ALTER mid-loop (catalog changes under the cursor) - snapshot into a temp table first. (b) Postgres renders a wrapped call as "( SELECT f() AS f )", so literal-string bare-detection false-positives - use regexp_count(total) > regexp_count(select-prefixed). (8) /requests bounded queries - was select\* unbounded + ?mine filtered in JS = silent 1000-row PostgREST truncation + mine-after-cap drop; split pending/decided, ?mine as DB predicate, decided capped explicitly at 500. (9) pgTAP pin of the no-JWT NULL-deny invariant (appsheet_writer/anon/future-AI-role all depend on current_user_role() returning NULL with no sub). DEFERRED (own units, see review doc): AI access contract (CRITICAL - agents must use authenticated RLS context not admin.ts), semantic/analytics views, ai_insights landing table, evidence-log partitioning, pgvector semantic layer; + multi-tenant org_id seam (before customer #2), /requests keyset paging, photo_markups SECURITY DEFINER helper. Caveat: eval-once win EXPLAIN-verified (InitPlan) not load-benchmarked; partition urgency volume-dependent (unmeasured).

## Spec 79 Б─■ Project metadata + client information (2026-06-13, COMPLETE units 1-3)

Operator asked "where do users set project/client info, what would help". Read-only design workflow (5 agents) mapped the gap: projects had only code/name/status/notes, NO client concept. Operator scope decisions (AskUserQuestion): client = reusable MASTER table (mirrors contractors/suppliers ADR 0033/0038), not inline; project fields = site_address, contract_reference (immutable like code), start_date, planned_completion_date, project_lead_id (INTERNAL person-in-charge, distinct from client.contact_person), project_type (enum, 6 operator-chosen Thai categories), budget_amount_thb (MONEY). Internal team/supervisors split to SPEC 80 (join table). **Unit 1 SHIPPED (1317a86, migrations 20260626000000/000100/000200 applied to prod under the db:push gate, pgTAP 897/0):** clients master (staff SELECT, PM/super INSERT/UPDATE created_by-pinned, no delete) + projects +8 cols + set_project_client RPC + update_project_settings extended 4-argБ├▓10-arg. MONEY posture: budget SELECT revoked from authenticated Б─■ but a COLUMN revoke was inert because authenticated holds a TABLE-level SELECT grant (the spec-46 C3 reality), so 000200 replaced it with explicit per-column grants excluding budget (MAINTENANCE: new projects columns must be added to that grant; money cols intentionally omitted). 000200 also wrapped current_user_role() in the clients policies in (select Б─╕) Б─■ the eval-once doctrine (file 40) now FAILS on any bare call, caught it on first db:test. validators + PROJECT_TYPE_LABEL + 18 unit tests + compile-time drift guard (tuple vs generated enum) + pgTAP file 42 (32 asserts) + file 32 signature pin updated. **Unit 2 SHIPPED (ca8c4cd):** settings form (/sa/projects/[id]/settings, PM/super) edits all fields + inline "Ю╧─Ю╦·Ю╦╢Ю╧┬Ю╦║Ю╦╔Ю╦╧Ю╦│Ю╦└Ю╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╧┐Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╧┬" (createClient mirrors masters); budget + staff roster read via admin client (budget revoked; users RLS read-self), clients via user session; contract_reference read-only. LESSONS: (a) exactOptionalPropertyTypes forbids passing `undefined` to an optional RPC arg Б─■ build the args object and OMIT unset keys (absent = SQL default null = COALESCE-preserve). (b) set_project_client p_client_id has no DEFAULT so typegen types it `string` (non-null); cast to pass null (clears) Б─■ or add DEFAULT NULL like spec-31 did. 653 unit / typecheck / lint / build green. **Unit 3 SHIPPED (399df41):** display Б─■ project detail header shows client/Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╦°Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╦┼Ю╦╜Ю╦  (display-name resolved via admin)/type/site lines (each only when set); /pm/projects list shows client name (one batched lookup); PDF report header (fast-path src/lib/reports/build-pdf) prints client name + mailing_address + site_address, suppressed when absent so legacy projects keep the old code/name/Generated header (worker/ stays frozen Б├▓ renders old header; atrophy-retired). No DB change Б├▓ no gate. 653 unit/typecheck/lint/build green. **SPEC 79 COMPLETE.** REMAINING: only SPEC 80 (project_members team join table). Seams recorded in spec 79 б╖Out-of-scope: /pm/clients management page, budget-vs-spend dashboard, clearing date/lead/type/budget back to null (COALESCE preserves), procurement client access. OPERATOR OWES (acceptance): open a project's settings as PM Б├▓ set site/dates/type/lead/budget, add+assign a client; confirm SA cannot reach settings or see budget.

## Spec 80 Б─■ Project team / supervisors (2026-06-13, SHIPPED)

The team list spec 79 split out. **SHIPPED (0902d07, migration 20260626000300 applied to prod under the db:push gate, pgTAP file 43, suite 911/0):** project_members join table (project_id, user_id, added_by, added_at; PK(project_id,user_id); user_id index) Б─■ mirrors work_package_members (ADR 0032) but MUTABLE (DELETE granted) and with eval-once-WRAPPED policies from the start (learned from spec-79: a bare current_user_role()/auth.uid() fails file 40; file 40 globally covers project_members so file 43 dropped its own redundant eval-once assert). RLS: staff SELECT, PM/super INSERT (added_by=(select auth.uid()) pinned) + DELETE; procurement excluded. No SECURITY DEFINER RPC Б─■ PM/super write directly under the authenticated session (they hold the grant+policy). App: addProjectMember (idempotent Б─■ 23505 = already member = ok) / removeProjectMember server actions (PM/super gate); settings-form Ю╦≈Ю╦╣Ю╦║Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥ section (list + Б°∙ remove + staff picker to add; add/remove persist immediately via their own actions + update LOCAL state with NO router.refresh so the main form's unsaved edits survive Б─■ same pattern as the inline client-add); project detail header shows a Ю╦≈Ю╦╣Ю╦║Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥ line (member names, admin-resolved alongside the lead in one fetchDisplayNames). project_lead_id (single lead, spec 79) stays distinct. LESSONS: (a) an RLS DELETE with a failing USING deletes 0 rows SILENTLY Б─■ no 42501 (only INSERT WITH CHECK throws); test the no-op (rows survive), not throws_ok. (b) the hand-rolled bare-call regex must be case-INSENSITIVE Б─■ Postgres renders the wrapped form as "( SELECT current_user_role() Б─╕)" uppercase, so a lowercase `!~ 'select Б─╕'` false-positives (use file 40's proven global check instead of re-rolling). 653 unit/typecheck/lint/build green. SEAMS (spec 80 б╖Out-of-scope): per-member role/title, team on the PDF/list (header-only v1), notify-on-add. OPERATOR OWES (acceptance): on a project's settings, add + remove a team member; the header shows Ю╦≈Ю╦╣Ю╦║Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥; a duplicate add is a no-op; SA cannot reach settings.

## Spec 81 Б─■ Master data management: clients б╥ suppliers б╥ contractors (2026-06-14, SHIPPED)

Operator picked this from a "what next" menu (build the master-data **screens** + unblock the deferred `suppliers.note`/`contractors.note`). **SHIPPED (migration 20260627000000_masters_notes.sql applied to prod under the db:push gate, pgTAP 935/0):** one PM-gated route `/pm/masters` with a RadioChip segmented control (Ю╦╔Ю╦╧Ю╦│Ю╦└Ю╧┴Ю╦╡/Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦┌Ю╦╡Ю╦╒/Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡) over the three reference masters Б─■ each created inline elsewhere and never editable until now (a name typo on a master that snapshots onto reports/PRs was permanent). Mirrors the `/workers` roster precedent minus the money machinery (no master has a rate/cost column, so reads use the ordinary user-session server client Б─■ no admin client).

**Notes-everywhere reaches the masters.** Migration adds `note text` + `CHECK(<=2000)` + `grant insert/update (note)` + a column comment to clients, suppliers, contractors. App cap 1000 (`validateNotes`), DB CHECK 2000 (specs 71Б─⌠75 doctrine). **No RLS policy dropped/created** Б─■ the note rides each table's existing UPDATE/INSERT policy, so the eval-once doctrine (pgTAP file 40) is untouched (this is exactly why a note column needs no RPC: it rides the existing policy). suppliers.note/contractors.note were DEFERRED in specs 74/75 for lack of an edit screen; spec 81 builds the screen, so they land here. Notes-everywhere now covers WP/projects/PR/labor/workers + clients/suppliers/contractors.

**No SECURITY DEFINER RPC.** `/pm/masters` is `requireRole(PM_ROLES)`-gated and PM/super already hold the INSERT/UPDATE policy + column grants on all three (clients pm/super; contractors sa/pm/superБ┼┤pm/super; suppliers pm/procurement/superБ┼┤pm/super), so the six actions (`{create,update}{Client,Supplier,Contractor}Record` in `src/app/pm/masters/actions.ts`) write directly under the authenticated session Б─■ the spec-80 project_members precedent. Each action re-checks PM_ROLES before the write: defense-in-depth + a real error, because an RLS UPDATE whose USING fails affects 0 rows SILENTLY (spec-80 lesson) and trusting RLS alone would mask a forbidden edit as success. Update sends only changed keys (omitted=preserve, ""=clear); `norm()` blanksБ├▓null. The existing inline quick-adds (createClient in settings, createSupplier in requests, createContractor in WP assignment) are UNTOUCHED Б─■ they stay note-less and return the new id for immediate selection in their host flow (recorded simplify-seam: a shared insert core could unify them; they differ in return shape, revalidate target, and note support).

**Components.** `master-manager.tsx` Б─■ generic presentational manager driven by a `MasterFieldDef[]` schema (key/label/type text|tel|email|textarea/maxLength); add card + per-row Ю╧│Ю╦│Ю╧┴Ю╧└Ю╦┌ expander; entity actions injected as `onCreate`/`onUpdate` (no server fn imported here Б─■ the NotesField pattern; toast on success spec 76; `active:` press tints spec 77). `masters-tabs.tsx` Б─■ the segmented-control shell, holds the active tab + binds the field-recordБ├▓typed-action mappers. `page.tsx` fetches all three lists (user session, `order by name`) Б├▓ MasterRow[] (snakeБ├▓camel) Б├▓ MastersTabs; +loading.tsx. Nav: `PM_HUB_NAV` += Ю╦┌Ю╧┴Ю╦╜Ю╦║Ю╦╧Ю╦╔Ю╦╚Ю╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦│ (5 items, desktop strip; no phone bottom-tab entry Б─■ same seam as /workers, /pm/payroll). site-map.md + feature-specs README (79/80/81 added) updated same-unit.

**Method/tests:** TDD RED-first `master-manager.test.tsx` (5: row render, textarea for textarea-type, onCreate with values, onUpdate with only-changed, error render). hub-nav pin bumped to 5 items. pgTAP +24 across files 24/26/42 (each +note column exists/nullable/text, +CHECK>2000 rejected, +has_column_privilege insert/update, +PM note update lands + outcome). database.types.ts hand-extended then `db:types` regen reconciled byte-EXACT (9 insertions / 0 deletions). LESSON: `pick()` union-spread helper keeps the field-recordБ├▓typed-action mapping exactOptionalPropertyTypes-clean (only present keys forwarded). Suites: 658 unit / 935 pgTAP / lint / typecheck / build green.

**OPERATOR OWES (acceptance):** as PM open `/pm/masters` Б├▓ three tabs; add a client with a note, edit it, reload Б├▓ persists; rename a supplier; rename a contractor; add a contractor note; confirm SA cannot reach `/pm/masters`. **SEAMS (recorded):** SA/procurement access to the management page (role-widening units); delete/merge/dedup (ADR 0033/0038 keep masters un-deletable); unify masters-page create with the inline quick-adds; per-record usage view (which projects/WPs/PRs reference a master); client budget/analytics (spec 79 seam).

## Spec 85 Б─■ Contacts v2 Unit 3: bank info, money-isolated (2026-06-14, SHIPPED)

## Spec 95 Б─■ iOS keyboard repaint guard (2026-06-15, SHIPPED, code-only)

Operator phone (WP page screenshot): "whenever user finished typing something and lower down keyboard, a part of screen will go missing, and cannot scroll to top." The spec-64 "keyboard case = next suspect." **ROUND 1 (309a245) shipped on the WRONG hypothesis** Б─■ assumed iOS scrolled the locked DOCUMENT and reset it to 0; operator: "not fixed." **Round-2 diagnosis (AskUserQuestion):** the screen RECOVERS ON ITS OWN the moment you scroll, and Ю╦ёЮ╦╣Ю╧─Ю╦÷Ю╦ёЮ╦┼ clears it Б├▓ it's a missing-REPAINT glitch, NOT a stuck scroll position. With the body LOCKED (overflow:hidden; PageShell's `<main>` the only scroller), iOS standalone WebKit resizes the viewport back when the keyboard closes but does NOT repaint the locked scroller Б─■ content (sticky header included) present but blank until a scroll forces a repaint. **FIX (round 2):** `ViewportScrollGuard` now reproduces the recovering scroll the instant the keyboard closes Б─■ `scroller.scrollBy(0,1)` then `scrollBy(0,-1)` next animation frame (position-preserving repaint nudge), on the `<main>` scroller. Same triggers (visualViewport `resize` back to ~full; `focusout` fallback) + same guard (skip while another editable is focused). No document-scroll reset (the position was never the problem). spec-64 body-lock + PageShell unchanged. interactive-widget viewport hint NOT used (iOS Safari doesn't honour it). TDD: tests/unit/viewport-scroll-guard.test.tsx (nudges scroller on blur with nothing focused; does NOT nudge while another field is focused). lint / typecheck / build green. Spec: docs/feature-specs/95-ios-keyboard-scroll-guard.md. LESSON: "blank area that recovers on scroll" = iOS missing-repaint after viewport resize, not a scroll offset Б─■ force a repaint (scroll nudge), don't reset position. Acceptance = operator iPhone (PWA: close/reopen or Ю╦ёЮ╦╣Ю╧─Ю╦÷Ю╦ёЮ╦┼ after deploy).

## Spec 99 Б─■ Split Contacts into three groups (2026-06-15, SHIPPED, code-only)

Operator: "Ю╦∙Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╦∙Ю╧┬Ю╦╜ is quite packed, do you think it's better to separate out clients and suppliers?"
The old /contacts crammed FIVE tabs (Ю╦╔Ю╦╧Ю╦│Ю╦└Ю╧┴Ю╦╡/Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦┌Ю╦╡Ю╦╒/Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡/DC/Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╧┐Ю╦╚Ю╧┴Ю╦ Ю╦ёЮ╦╢Ю╦│Ю╦╡Ю╦ё) into one screen, with the
status filter showing on only three of them = packed + inconsistent. AskUserQuestion Б├▓ operator chose
**three groups** (over "crews vs business orgs" two-way or "clients-only"): Ю╦╔Ю╦╧Ю╦│Ю╦└Ю╧┴Ю╦╡ | Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦┌Ю╦╡Ю╦╒+Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╧┐Ю╦╚Ю╧┴Ю╦ Ю╦ёЮ╦╢Ю╦│Ю╦╡Ю╦ё
(vendors you pay) | Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╧─Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦╡+DC (labor crews). Placement = three entries under Ю╦∙Ю╦╠Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦└Ю╧┬Ю╦╡ Б─╨ Ю╦┌Ю╧┴Ю╦╜Ю╦║Ю╦╧Ю╦╔Ю╦╚Ю╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦│,

## Spec 112 Б─■ Band-relative row health color in the procurement grid (2026-06-15, SHIPPED, code-only)

Operator pushed back on naive grid coloring: "coloring urgent red doesn't help if they already
ordered the things Б─■ design better, think outside the box, ultrathink." KEY REFRAME: request
priority is the REQUESTER's lens, stale once ordered; the buyer's grid color should encode the
BUYER's TIME pressure, **band-relative** (red MEANS a different thing per band). **AskUserQuestion:
"band-relative health RAG"** (over late-only / buyer-SLA-aging). App-only, no DB. **SHIPPED:** (1)
pure `lib/purchasing/row-health.ts` (TDD, +14 unit) Б─■ `rowHealth(status, eta, neededBy, todayIso)` Б├▓
late|at_risk|on_track|waiting, band-aware via procurementBand: **to_order** (not ordered) pressure =
needed_by (pastБ├▓late, Б┴╓7dБ├▓at_risk, else on_track, no-needБ├▓on_track); **in_transit** (ordered) = ETA
pastБ├▓late, ETA>needed_byБ├▓at_risk (lands late), else on_track, no-etaБ├▓on_track (request urgency
IRRELEVANT here Б─■ the operator's whole point, so rowHealth takes NO priority input); **received**Б├▓
on_track; **awaiting_approval/rejected/cancelled**Б├▓waiting (not the buyer's move). `HEALTH_SOON_DAYS=7`;
`daysUntil` = UTC-midnight ISO diff (tz-stable). +`rowHealthLabel` Thai (hover title). (2) grid: each
data row's FIRST cell gets `border-l-4` + a health color (late=danger, at_risk=attn, on_track=
done-strong, waiting=edge) + `title` reason; ETA turns text-danger when late. Used all-sides color
tokens (border-danger etc.) NOT border-l-<token> (don't rely on left-specific color generation). (3)
`/requests` passes `today=bangkokTodayISO()` into the grid so health uses the Bangkok civil date, not
the client clock. **Three orthogonal grid signals now:** band=action б╥ mini-bar=stage б╥ color=on-time.
Grid only Б─■ pill/mini-bar/cards/band-header unchanged. 825 unit / lint / typecheck / build green; **no
migration Б├▓ pgTAP 1025 untouched**. Spec: docs/feature-specs/112-grid-row-health-color.md. **NOT
preview-verified** (procurement-gated) Б├▓ acceptance = procurement user PC: not-ordered-past-needed_by
glows red, shipment-past-ETA red, shipment-landing-after-need amber, on-track green, awaiting neutral;
hover explains. SEAMS: SOON window fixed at 7d (no per-project SLA); receivedБ├▓amber on missing invoice
(filing gap) needs attachment query Б─■ deferred; color legend + health on phone cards later; in_transit
no-ETA reads on_track (an "unmanaged PO" amber is a later refinement).

## ADR 0044 + Spec 115 Б─■ Purchase orders (grouping tickets) Б─■ DESIGN LOCKED, build pending (2026-06-16)

Operator asked how admins handle a purchase covering **more than one ticket** + partial delivery.
Found the gap: the only procurement entity is `purchase_requests` (one ticket = one line/WP/qty,
atomic delivery) Б─■ **no PO object**; a buyer ordering 5 tickets from one supplier records 5ц≈, and the
per-ticket amount means one invoice total is split by hand. Partial-**across**-tickets already works
(each ticket delivers independently) but ungrouped; partial-**within**-a-ticket (split qty) is
unmodelled (a later receipts unit). Two AskUserQuestions locked the design: **(1) build PO grouping**
(over partial-receipts / both / workaround); **(2) per-ticket prices** (PO total = sum, over
PO-total-+-split / lump) Б─■ preserves per-WP material spend (specs 100/103/106 read amount per ticket).
**ADR 0044 (Accepted)** + **spec 115** written: new `purchase_orders` table (po_number seq, supplier_id
FK + snapshot, eta, ordered_at, notes, created_by; **no money column** Б─■ total is computed);
`purchase_requests.purchase_order_id` nullable FK; **atomic SECURITY DEFINER `create_purchase_order`**
(back-office gate on the AUTHENTICATED session per the spec-68 lesson; per-line guard status=approved Б├▓
amount/supplier/eta/purchased_at/status=purchased/po_id; audit per line + PO row); ship+delivery stay
per-ticket (partial-across works); **PO status DERIVED** (openБ├▓orderedБ├▓partially_receivedБ├▓received,
pure helper, not stored); RLS = back-office SELECT (ADR 0026), RPC-only writer (ADR 0038 posture).
**Phased build: spec 115 = data layer** (table+FK+RLS+RPC+helpers+pgTAP+types, schema Б├▓ operator gate);
**spec 116 = UI** (grid multi-select bundling, create-PO form w/ per-line prices, grouped display, PO
context in the drawer). NOT YET BUILT Б─■ schema migration is the riskiest change type (immutable once
merged); building it deliberately. SEAMS: within-ticket partial receipts, PO line-set editing, PO PDF.
Also still open: delete the 7 test PRs (2926Б─⌠2932) + the /grid-preview page after operator review.

---

## Spec 115 Б─■ Purchase orders: data layer (ADR 0044, phase 1) Б─■ SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** the PO grouping data layer. Migrations `20260701000000` (audit_action `+purchase_order_create`,
own txn Б─■ ADD VALUE can't be used same-txn) + `20260701000100` (table + FK + RLS + RPC) applied to prod
under the operator gate. **No UI** (that's spec 116).

- **`purchase_orders` table:** `po_number` own sequence (mirrors `pr_number`), `supplier_id` FK + `supplier`
  text snapshot (spec-33 pattern), `eta`, `ordered_at`, `notes` CHECK(Б┴╓2000), `created_by`, timestamps.
  **NO money column** (б╖3) Б─■ the PO total is the computed SUM of member `purchase_requests.amount`, so per-WP
  material spend (specs 100/103/106) stays exact. RLS: back-office SELECT site-wide (site_admin/PM/procurement/
  super, ADR 0026, eval-once wrapped); **NO INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE policy** Б─■ the RPC (function owner) is the
  only writer (ADR 0038). `grant select` to authenticated only; appsheet_writer unaffected.
- **`purchase_requests.purchase_order_id`** nullable FK Б├▓ `purchase_orders(id)` (б╖2). RPC-only-writable: the
  column-scoped authenticated UPDATE grant (20260616000400) doesn't name it, so app sessions can't set it
  directly. Indexed (PO Б├▓ members read). `purchase_orders.supplier_id` also indexed.
- **`create_purchase_order(p_supplier_id uuid, p_eta date, p_lines jsonb)`** SECURITY DEFINER, search_path
  pinned, returns the new PO id (uuid). Back-office gate on the **authenticated session** (spec-68 lesson Б─■
  service-role has no JWT so auth.uid()/current_user_role() would refuse it; grant execute to authenticated,
  revoke from public/anon). Inserts the PO; per line `{request_id, amount}` guards `status='approved'` then
  stamps amount/supplier(snapshot)/eta/purchased_at=now()/status='purchased'/purchase_order_id. **All-or-
  nothing** (one txn Б─■ a non-approved line rolls back the whole bundle). Audit: the per-line approvedБ├▓purchased
  UPDATE fires the **existing** `purchase_requests_audit_appsheet` trigger Б├▓ one `purchase_request_purchase`
  row per line (mirrors record_purchase, null-actor/principal=authenticated); the RPC writes ONE additional
  `purchase_order_create` row carrying the real actor + po_number/supplier/eta/request_ids.
- **Pure helpers** `src/lib/purchasing/purchase-order.ts` (TDD-first, 10 unit): `derivePurchaseOrderStatus`
  (openБ├▓orderedБ├▓partially_receivedБ├▓received; on_route counts as ordered; rejected/cancelled EXCLUDED;
  empty roll-up Б├▓ open) + `purchaseOrderTotal` (sum of non-null line amounts).
- **pgTAP file 49** (+48): catalog/columns/notes-CHECK/RLS posture (1 SELECT policy, no write policy, no
  authenticated INSERT/UPDATE)/member FK; RPC signature (SECURITY DEFINER + search_path + returns uuid +
  authenticated-only execute) + behaviour (bundles approved Б├▓ purchased/priced/stamped/snapshotted; sums 300;
  PO-create + 2 per-line purchase audit rows; refuses non-approved line / empty set / unknown supplier; atomic
  rollback). Enum pins updated in files 03 + 18 (grep-all-enum-pins lesson).
- **database.types.ts** hand-extended then `db:types` reconciled Б─■ content byte-identical (only delta was the
  `purchase_orders` block ordering; Supabase sorts it before `purchase_requests`).

**Gate honored:** built local-green (lint / typecheck / 842 unit / build), AskUserQuestion Б├▓ "Apply now" Б├▓
db:push (migration FIRST), db:types reconcile, db:test 1073/0-fail, THEN commit + push. **Suites:** 842 unit /
1073 pgTAP.

**Acceptance (no UI):** `create_purchase_order` bundles approved tickets into a PO (each line Б├▓ purchased,
priced, stamped), refuses a non-approved line, is back-office-gated; per-WP spend still reads each line's
amount; pgTAP green. **Next:** spec 116 = the UI (grid multi-select bundling, create-PO form with per-line
prices, grouped display, PO context in the review drawer). Out (later units): within-ticket partial receipts
(split qty), PO line-set editing, PO PDF.

**Still open (test artifacts, delete on operator's "done reviewing"):** the 7 seeded test PRs
(`delete from public.purchase_requests where pr_number between 2926 and 2932;`) + the temporary
`src/app/grid-preview/page.tsx` (spec 113) + its `nav-back-affordance.test.ts` EXCLUDED_ROUTES entry.

## Spec 116 Б─■ Purchase orders: create-PO UI (ADR 0044, phase 2) Б─■ SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** the screen to actually create a multi-ticket PO (spec 115 shipped only the engine). On the
procurement desktop grid, the buyer checks several **approved** (`to_order`) tickets Б├▓ a sticky
`Ю╦╙Ю╦ёЮ╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦┤ PO (n)` bar Б├▓ a bottom-sheet form (supplier picker + ETA + per-line price inputs + live total) Б├▓
`createPurchaseOrder` action Б├▓ the `create_purchase_order` RPC bundles them atomically. **No schema**
(pure UI on the spec-115 data layer).

- **Pure validator** `src/lib/purchasing/validate-create-purchase-order.ts` (TDD, 8 unit): Б┴╔1 line, a
  supplier UUID, each amount null-or-positive, no duplicate request ids, and a **required** valid ETA
  (deliberate Б─■ a PO commits a delivery date; ad-hoc `record_purchase` stays ETA-optional. Optional-PO-
  ETA is a recorded seam needing the RPC's `p_eta` to gain a SQL default first).
- **Server action** `createPurchaseOrder({ supplierId, eta, lines })` in `src/app/requests/actions.ts`
  Б─■ runs on the **authenticated user session** (`getActionUser`, NOT the admin client, because the RPC
  is role-gated on `current_user_role()`); calls `supabase.rpc("create_purchase_order", Б─╕)`, maps
  42501/P0001 to Thai, `revalidatePath("/requests")`, returns `{ ok, poId }`.
- **`CreatePurchaseOrderSheet`** (`src/components/features/create-purchase-order-sheet.tsx`, client):
  supplier `<select>`, ETA date, per-line price inputs, live total via `purchaseOrderTotal`. Submit Б├▓
  action Б├▓ on success clears the selection, closes, `router.refresh()` (bundled rows leave `to_order`,
  appear in `in_transit`). Component test (4): renders lines + live total, submits the right payload,
  surfaces errors, rejects a bad price client-side.
- **`procurement-grid.tsx`**: a checkbox on each approved (`to_order`) row + the sticky bundle bar +
  the sheet Б─■ **all gated on `canBundle` (suppliers present)**, so the spec-113 preview/smoke (no
  suppliers) stays selection-free and router-free.

**LESSON (the smoke test earned its keep):** `ProcurementGrid` initially mounted `CreatePurchaseOrderSheet`
unconditionally; the sheet's top-level `useRouter()` threw "app router not mounted" in the no-router
smoke test. Gating the mount on `canBundle` fixed it Б─■ a component that calls `useRouter` must not be
mounted on a surface that has no router (preview/smoke). All create-PO props are clientБ├▓client (the
Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦┌Ю╦╡Ю╦╒ serverБ├▓client function-prop lesson does not bite here).

**Gate:** 860 unit / lint / typecheck / build green. No schema Б├▓ no operator gate; committed + pushed.
**Acceptance** (procurement can't be preview-verified Б─■ preview only renders `/login`): a procurement
user (Pattrawut) on a PC checks 2+ approved tickets Б├▓ Ю╦╙Ю╦ёЮ╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦┤ PO Б├▓ supplier + ETA + prices Б├▓ creates the
PO; tickets become purchased/priced/stamped and leave the to-order band.

**OUT (deferred follow-ups):** grouped PO display (a PO + its members as a group) + PO context in the
review drawer; PO line-set editing; PO PDF; phone multi-select; optional-PO-ETA. Also still queued: the
**documents+photos attachments** unit the operator asked for (Q1 answered = documents + photos; build
after this).

---

## Spec 117 Б─■ Create-PO UX round (mockup-approved) Б─■ SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** operator said "think hard about the UXUI" on the spec-116 create-PO flow. Since procurement
routes can't be preview-verified (preview only renders `/login`), a hard critique found real defects, a
visualize **mockup** was built, and the operator approved "build the full redesign." Seven UI fixes (no
schema):

1. **Right-side panel, not a bottom sheet** Б─■ the form was a `BottomSheet` (phone idiom) on a
   desktop-only feature; switched to `side="right"` (matches the review drawer). 2. **Inline
   Ю╧─Ю╦·Ю╦╢Ю╧┬Ю╦║Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦┌Ю╦╡Ю╦╒Ю╧┐Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╧┬** (createSupplier) Б─■ no more dead-end when the supplier isn't listed. 3. **Required-ETA
   `Ю╦┬Ю╦ЁЮ╧─Ю╦⌡Ю╧┤Ю╦≥` badge + disabled-submit helper line** (explains why the button is off). 4. **Selected rows
   highlighted** (`bg-action-soft`) on the grid. 5. **Discoverability caption** above the grid
   (procurement). 6. **WP code per line** in the sheet (bundles can span projects). 7. **Success toast**
   (`useToast().success`) on create.

Files: `create-purchase-order-sheet.tsx` (rewritten), `procurement-grid.tsx` (highlight + caption +
`wp_code` into `CreatePoLine`), component test extended (+1 inline-add-supplier case, `createSupplier`
mock, `wp_code` fixtures). **TRAP fixed:** a `Ю╦┬Ю╦ЁЮ╧─Ю╦⌡Ю╧┤Ю╦≥` badge inside the ETA `<label>` would change its
accessible name and break `getByLabelText` Б─■ moved the badge to a sibling of the label. `useToast` is a
NO-OP outside its provider, so the test needs no toast mock.

**Gate:** unit / lint / typecheck / build green; no schema Б├▓ no operator gate; committed + pushed.
**Acceptance** = procurement (Pattrawut) on a PC: tick approved tickets (rows highlight) Б├▓ right-side
Ю╦╙Ю╦ёЮ╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦┤ PO panel Б├▓ add supplier inline / set required ETA / enter prices Б├▓ create Б├▓ success toast.

**METHOD note (reusable):** for an un-preview-verifiable surface, the right move on a "think about UX"
ask is a visualize mockup Б├▓ operator approval Б├▓ build (the spec-108 loop), NOT shipping blind UI then
hoping. The mockup is the verification the preview can't give.

## Spec 118 Б─■ Phone PO creation: the add-to-PO basket Б─■ SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** operator "what about on phone?" Б─■ specs 116/117 made PO creation desktop-only (grid is `lg:`).
Senior-designer pass (the uxui bundle): the real choice was the phone interaction MODEL; operator picked
the **basket** (browse Б├▓ add Б├▓ checkout) over worklist-tick / supplier-first, and approved a detailed
mockup before the build. SHIPPED (no schema).

- **`PhonePoBasket`** (client) renders the `to_order` band on phone as compact cards (item/PRб╥WPб╥qty/
  status, tap Б├▓ detail) each with a **Ю╧─Ю╦·Ю╦╢Ю╧┬Ю╦║Ю╧─Ю╦┌Ю╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╧┐Ю╦ Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜** toggle; added Б├▓ highlighted + **Ю╦╜Ю╦╒Ю╦╧Ю╧┬Ю╧┐Ю╦≥
  Ю╧┐Ю╦ Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜ б╥ Ю╧│Ю╦∙Ю╦╟Ю╧─Ю╦·Ю╦╥Ю╧┬Ю╦╜Ю╦≥Ю╦ЁЮ╦╜Ю╦╜Ю╦│**. A **floating basket bar** (`bg-fill`, fixed, `z-30`, `lg:hidden`) shows the
  running count **above the tab bar** (`bottom-[calc(4rem+env(safe-area-inset-bottom))] sm:bottom-4` Б─■
  phone has the 64px+safe tab bar, tablet doesn't) Б├▓ opens the checkout sheet.
- **Checkout** reuses `CreatePurchaseOrderSheet` at `side="bottom"` (the reason the bottom variant was
  kept when spec 117 moved desktop to `side="right"`) + a new optional `onRemoveLine` (per-line Б°∙ to
  drop a ticket; empties/closes on the last). Supplier+inline-add, required ETA, prices, total, success
  toast all inherited.
- **Page**: `/requests` phone block Б─■ `to_order` band Б├▓ `PhonePoBasket` when `canBundlePhone`
  (procurement + suppliers loaded); other bands keep `PurchaseRequestCard`; desktop keeps the grid.
  Reuses the serializable `ProcurementGridRecord` the grid builds.

**Test:** `phone-po-basket.test.tsx` (4) Б─■ add reveals the bar + count, bar opens the sheet, a line drops
from inside the sheet. **Gate:** unit / lint / typecheck / build green; no schema Б├▓ no gate; committed +
pushed. **Acceptance** = procurement (Pattrawut) on a **phone** (phone layout can't be preview-verified;
the bar/tab-bar offset is breakpoint-sensitive Б─■ operator-on-device).

**LESSON (layout, reusable):** the `lg:hidden` phone block spans BOTH phone (<640, fixed tab bar present)
and tablet (640Б─⌠1024, no tab bar Б─■ HubNav top strip instead). A bar pinned above the tab bar needs a
responsive offset (`bottom-[calc(4rem+safe)] sm:bottom-4`) or it floats with a gap on tablet. PageShell
`app` = `pb-20 sm:pb-0` (phone tab-bar clearance); add a spacer so a fixed bar never covers the last card.

## Spec 119 / ADR 0045 Б─■ VAT capture on purchases (phase 1) Б─■ SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** operator asked about partial delivery + VAT. **Partial delivery = CLOSED** (across-ticket
already works via the spec-115 PO roll-up; within-ticket split-quantity declined). **VAT** Б─■ operator:
"user can pick whether the price is inclusive or exclusive"; spend = GROSS. SHIPPED (migration
`20260701000200` applied to prod under the gate; 874 unit / 1075 pgTAP / lint / typecheck / build).

- **Model (ADR 0045):** `amount` is canonically the GROSS (what you pay; spend/budget/PO-total read it
  unchanged). New `purchase_requests.vat_rate numeric(5,2) default 0` (CHECK 0Б─⌠100); **net/VAT DERIVED**
  (`src/lib/purchasing/vat.ts`, TDD 8 unit: `deriveVatBreakdown` net+VAT sum back to gross;
  `grossFromEntry`; `rateForMode`; `VAT_RATE=7`). The mode (inclusive/exclusive/none) is an entry
  convenience Б─■ only gross + rate are stored.
- **Migration:** vat_rate column + the 3 amount-entry RPCs (`record_purchase`, `create_purchase_order`,
  `record_site_purchase`) DROP+CREATE with `+p_vat_rate` (default 0 Б├▓ existing callers/tests/appsheet
  unaffected; bodies reproduced verbatim + the rate). vat_rate = amount's posture (RPC-write, not in the
  authenticated UPDATE grant). RPC sig pins updated (files 26/33/49, +numeric). pgTAP file 49 +2.
- **UI (this push Б─■ PO checkout only):** `CreatePurchaseOrderSheet` gains a VAT mode picker; per-line
  prices resolve to gross via the mode; **live net/VAT/gross breakdown**; `createPurchaseOrder` passes
  `p_vat_rate` (one rate per PO). Sheet test +1 (exclusive Б├▓ +7%).

**Gate honored:** local-green Б├▓ "Apply now" Б├▓ db:push (migration first) Б├▓ db:types reconcile (content
byte-identical; only the `create_purchase_order` Args line reflowed) Б├▓ db:test 1075/0-fail Б├▓ commit+push.

**OUT (additive follow-ups Б─■ RPCs already accept the rate, NO further schema):** VAT picker on the
`record_purchase` + `record_site_purchase` forms; a **persistent net/VAT readout** on the request detail
page + the grid/drawer. **OUT (v3 accounting):** withholding tax, tax-invoice (Ю╧┐Ю╦ Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦│Ю╦╠Ю╦ Ю╦═Ю╦╡Ю╦╘Ю╦╣) docs, reports.

## Spec 120 Б─■ Unify purchase recording into PO creation Б─■ SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** operator Б─■ "replace Ю╦ Ю╦╠Ю╦≥Ю╦≈Ю╦╤Ю╦│Ю╦│Ю╦╡Ю╦ёЮ╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜ with the new PO creation." Two purchase paths had diverged
(spec-33 per-ticket `record_purchase` form vs the spec-116/119 PO flow); PO is the better-built one, so
it becomes the single path. SHIPPED (migration `20260701000300` applied to prod under the gate; 874 unit
/ 1076 pgTAP / lint / typecheck / build).

- **Single-ticket = a one-line PO.** On an approved request the inline record form Б├▓ a **"Ю╦╙Ю╦ёЮ╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦┤ PO"
  button that opens the create-PO sheet pre-seeded with that one ticket** (one tap, no grid hunting; VAT/
  supplier/ETA/price/order_ref all ride along). Detail page: `CreatePoFromRequestButton` (new client; the
  server page passes the serializable line + suppliers). Procurement drawer: the `record` action Б├▓ a
  button that closes the drawer, seeds the basket with that record, opens the grid's existing sheet (an
  `onCreatePo` callback threaded RecordReviewDrawer Б├▓ DrawerBody; `suppliers` dropped from that chain).
- **order_ref carried.** Migration DROP+CREATE `create_purchase_order` `+p_order_ref` (Б┴╓80, one per PO,
  written onto each member's existing `purchase_requests.order_ref` Б─■ NO new column). Sheet gains an
  optional order-ref field; action passes `p_order_ref`. (4th create_purchase_order revision today Б─■
  000100 Б├▓ +vat 000200 Б├▓ +order_ref 000300; each DROP+CREATE reproduces the prior body verbatim.)
- **`PurchaseRecordForm` retired from the UI** (both usages gone); the component file + the
  `record_purchase` RPC LEFT in place (AppSheet doesn't call the RPC; removal is a later cleanup).
  `SupplierOption` still lives in `purchase-record-form.tsx` as a type-only import.

**Gate honored:** local-green Б├▓ "Apply now" Б├▓ db:push Б├▓ db:types reconcile (IDENTICAL Б─■ hand-extension
exact) Б├▓ db:test 1076/0 Б├▓ commit + push. pgTAP file 49: order_ref stored + the sig pins (now
`(uuid,date,jsonb,numeric,text)`). Sheet test: order_ref in the payload.

**SESSION TOTAL (2026-06-16, EIGHT units, 5 prod migrations): 115 PO data layer б╥ Ю╦°Ю╦╧Ю╧┴Ю╦┌Ю╦╡Ю╦╒ fix б╥ 116 PO
create б╥ 117 create-PO UX б╥ 118 phone basket б╥ 119/ADR0045 VAT б╥ 120 unify-record-into-PO.** PO is now
THE purchase path (desktop + phone, VAT, order_ref). **Acceptance:** approved request Б├▓ Ю╦╙Ю╦ёЮ╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦┤ PO
pre-seeded Б├▓ one-line PO. **OUT (cleanup):** delete `PurchaseRecordForm` + the `record_purchase` RPC.

**Spec 120 review tweak (operator):** the VAT picker (a 3-option dropdown) Б├▓ the accessible `RadioChip`
segmented control (spec 67) with SHORT labels (Ю╦│Ю╧┬Ю╦╜Ю╦≥ VAT / Ю╦ёЮ╦╖Ю╦║ VAT Ю╧│Ю╦╔Ю╧┴Ю╦╖ / Ю╧└Ю╦║Ю╧┬Ю╦║Ю╦╣ VAT Б─■ the full phrases
would overflow the narrow sheet; the live net/VAT/gross line carries the precise meaning). **Default
flipped inclusive Б├▓ exclusive (Ю╦│Ю╧┬Ю╦╜Ю╦≥ VAT)** Б─■ a PO is created from a quotation, and Thai quotes are
usually quoted ex-VAT (net + 7%). Surfacing the mode as visible chips + the breakdown is the guard against
the exclusive-transform mis-entry. UI-only (no schema). Sheet test updated (default-exclusive amounts +
RadioChip selection). REUSABLE: Б┴╓4 fixed mutually-exclusive options that affect MONEY Б├▓ prefer a visible
RadioChip over a dropdown (the user picks deliberately, sees the effect), but keep labels short or it
overflows.

## Spec 121 Б─■ PDF support in purchasing attachments (ADR 0046 Layer A) Б─■ SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** the deferred documents+photos foundation. Purchasing attachments are image-only today
(`pr-attachments` bucket = jpeg/png/webp/heic, downscaled Б─■ spec 34). Layer A makes a **PDF** attachable

- viewable on the **existing** surfaces (invoice uploader + reference stager) Б─■ attach a PDF quote/
  invoice to a request. Layers B (PO-level source-doc + side-by-side create-PO surface) and C (AI
  extraction) are separate later units, untouched.

* **kind decision = new `'pdf'`** (over a non-downscale `image` branch): ADR 0046 names `kind image|pdf`;
  viewer dispatches cleanly on kind (iframe vs lightbox); `pra_purpose_kind` auto-blocks a PDF from a
  delivery-confirmation slot; the image-only token trigger skips PDFs; semantic honesty.
* **Migrations (operator-gated):** (1) re-assert `pr-attachments` `allowed_mime_types` += `application/pdf`
  (25 MiB cap stays) + `alter type Б─╕ add value 'pdf'` (no pdf-literal usage in the same file Б├▓
  same-txn-safe). (2) `pra_pdf_shape` CHECK (pdf content row carries `storage_path`, no `url`) Б─■ separate
  file because the CHECK _uses_ `'pdf'`.
* **No-downscale upload:** raw PDF bytes (`contentType: application/pdf`) to the canonical
  `.../{att}.pdf` path; metadata-after-upload (spec-24 pattern). PDFs NOT offline-queue-bracketed this
  unit (manual-retry, mirrors invoice uploader Б─■ recorded seam; `QueuedUpload.ext` stays `PhotoExt`).
* **Viewer:** `AttachmentPdf` (signed-URL `<iframe>` + open-in-new-tab); detail page groups by kind
  (reference images/PDFs/links; invoice images/PDFs); signed URLs minted for image + pdf rows.

**Money posture unchanged.** Gate honored: lint / typecheck / build / **881 unit** local-green Б├▓
AskUserQuestion "Apply now" Б├▓ db:push (migrations `20260702000000` + `20260702000100` applied to prod) Б├▓
db:types reconcile (**byte-identical** to the hand-extension) Б├▓ db:test **1081/0**. Then commit + push.

**Build notes (reusable):** (1) `buildPrAttachmentStoragePath` widened `PhotoExt` Б├▓ `AttachmentExt`
(`PhotoExt | "pdf"`) Б─■ its existing pin test asserted `pdf` Б├▓ null; flipped to assert it builds, added a
truly-invalid-ext case (TDD redБ├▓green anchor). (2) The detail page's reference grouping used
`kind !== "image"` for links Б─■ a pdf would have leaked into the link list (and been dropped, url=null);
fixed to `kind === "link"` + a new `referencePdfs`/`invoicePdfs` split. (3) Signed-URL minting widened
to `image || pdf` rows (pdfs were getting no URL). (4) Server actions derive the stored kind from the
validated ext (`attachmentKindForExt`) Б─■ client-passed kind is not trusted; `findLandedAttachment` now
pins the actual kind (image-only check would mis-replay a pdf). (5) `addDeliveryConfirmationPhoto` stays
image-only on purpose (a receipt photo; `pra_purpose_kind` enforces). **Acceptance owed:** procurement/
back-office user attaches a PDF quote/invoice on `/requests/[id]` Б├▓ uploads un-downscaled + renders in
the iframe viewer; images still work. (Auth-gated route Б├▓ operator-on-live, not preview-verifiable.)
**Recorded seam:** PDF reference attachments are NOT offline-queue-bracketed (manual-retry, mirrors the
invoice uploader; `QueuedUpload.ext` stays `PhotoExt`). **NEXT:** ADR 0046 Layer B (document-first
create-PO: PO-level source-doc + side-by-side surface) Б├▓ Layer C (AI extraction, Claude).

## Spec 125 Б─■ PO source-document attachments (ADR 0046 Layer B, Unit 1) Б─■ SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** the quotation/invoice a PO is created from now attaches at the **PO level** (ADR 0046
decision 2). Operator picked the **phased "attach-doc first"** cut: this unit = data layer + a doc picker
in the **existing** create-PO sheet (uploaded when the PO is created) + a viewer on the request detail
page. The full **side-by-side wide doc|form surface** (ADR 0046 decision 4) is the next unit.

- **Decisions** (ADR 0046 left these "to decide at spec time"): grain = a **`purchase_order_attachments`
  table** (mirrors pr_attachments; append-only + tombstone-ready; kind image|pdf; **no `purpose` column**
  v1 Б─■ every PO doc is the source doc, YAGNI; **no token side-table** Б─■ vestigial AppSheet bridge).
  Storage = a **new private `po-attachments` bucket** (image + application/pdf from day one Б─■ the Layer A
  lesson), path `{po_id}/{att}.{ext}` (a PO spans projects Б├▓ po_id is the scope). Writer = **direct INSERT
  under RLS** (mirror pr_attachments), **content rows only** (no tombstone arm/removal UI v1).
- **Upload-on-submit** (ADR 0046 decision 3, resolves the no-po_id-yet chicken-and-egg): the sheet keeps
  the file client-side; `createPurchaseOrder` returns `poId` Б├▓ browser uploads to `po-attachments/{poId}/Б─╕`
  Б├▓ `addPurchaseOrderAttachment` records the row. PDFs raw (no spec-34 downscale), images prepared. A
  failed doc upload is **non-fatal** (the PO stands; the doc is optional) Б─■ toast warns; no re-attach
  surface until the PO-doc page lands (recorded seam).
- **Viewer:** the PR detail page (`/requests/[id]`) shows the PO's source doc when the ticket has a
  `purchase_order_id` (there's no PO detail page yet) Б─■ reuses the Layer A `AttachmentPdf` / `ZoomablePhoto`.

**Money posture unchanged.** Gate honored: lint / typecheck / build / **885 unit** local-green Б├▓
AskUserQuestion "Apply now" Б├▓ db:push (`20260703000000` table+bucket; **`20260703000100` fix-forward**) Б├▓
db:types reconcile (content byte-identical; only view-block ordering differed, regen committed) Б├▓ db:test
**1104/0**.

**KEY LESSON (reusable):** the new RLS policies first shipped with **bare** `current_user_role()` /
`auth.uid()` (I mirrored pr_attachments' migration SOURCE, which predates the rank-3 eval-once hardening Б─■
the LIVE policies were since wrapped). **db:test file 40 (rls-eval-once) caught it** (2 failures) Б├▓ a
fix-forward migration (`20260703000100`) DROP+CREATEs both policies wrapped in `(select Б─╕)`. **Any NEW
public RLS policy must wrap auth calls in `(select Б─╕)` from the start** Б─■ don't copy a pre-2026-06-25
migration's bare form. **Acceptance owed:** procurement user creates a PO + attaches a PDF/photo quote Б├▓
PO created, doc saved; any member ticket's detail page shows the source doc. (Procurement-gated route Б├▓
operator-on-live.) **NEXT:** ADR 0046 Layer B Unit 2 (the side-by-side wide create-PO surface) Б├▓ Layer C
(AI extraction). Seams: PO-doc removal/replace UI; multi-doc + quote/invoice `purpose` split; PO detail page.

## Spec 126 Б─■ Document-first create-PO surface (ADR 0046 Layer B, Unit 2) Б─■ SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** the attached quote/invoice is now a **readable reference while filling the PO** (ADR 0046
decision 4). Spec 125 added the doc picker + upload-on-submit (filename chip only); this makes the doc
preview side-by-side. **Operator decisions** (AskUserQuestion, after a visualize mockup Б─■ the right move
for an un-preview-verifiable procurement+lg surface): container = **wide modal** (over a dedicated route Б─■
preserves the in-memory ticket selection from all 3 entry points); flow = **attach-inside-expands**.
**NO schema** (pure UI on Unit 1's table/bucket/action) Б├▓ no operator gate.

- `BottomSheet` gains **`wide?`** Б─■ the RIGHT panel grows `max-w-md Б├▓ lg:max-w-5xl` (no effect on the
  bottom variant). Create-PO sheet passes `wide={docFile != null}`.
- **Client object-URL preview** (ADR 0046 decision 3 Б─■ no upload while filling): PDF via `<iframe>`,
  image via `<img>` on a `blob:` URL (revoked on change/unmount); bytes still upload on submit (spec 125).
- **Split on lg+, toggle on phone:** doc attached Б├▓ 2-col `lg:grid-cols-[3fr_2fr]` (doc left, form right);
  below `lg` a Ю╧─Ю╦╜Ю╦│Ю╦╙Ю╦╡Ю╦ёБ┤└Ю╦÷Ю╦╜Ю╦ёЮ╧▄Ю╦║ toggle (`hidden lg:block` swap, fresh attach lands on Ю╧─Ю╦╜Ю╦│Ю╦╙Ю╦╡Ю╦ё). No doc Б├▓ the
  plain single-column form + an attach button; the attach affordance (Ю╧─Ю╦⌡Ю╦╢Ю╦■/Ю╧─Ю╦⌡Ю╦╔Ю╦╣Ю╧┬Ю╦╒Ю╦≥/Ю╦≥Ю╦ЁЮ╦╜Ю╦╜Ю╦│) moves into the
  doc pane once a doc is present. All 3 entry points inherit it (shared sheet; sheet is always `side="right"`).

**Gate:** lint / typecheck / build / **885 unit** green; no schema Б├▓ no db:push, pgTAP unchanged (1104);
committed + pushed. **Acceptance** (procurement, lg-only, not preview-verifiable Б├▓ operator-on-live): open

## Spec 131 U1 - DC onboarding packet: data layer (2026-06-16)

Status: COMPLETE Б─■ 2026-06-16. Migrations applied to prod; pgTAP **56 files / 1215 asserts / 0 failures**; lint clean б╥ 925 unit green б╥ build green б╥ types reconciled. (pgTAP caught a real security bug, fixed-forward in `20260709000200`: the consent RPCs' self-check `v_is_self := current_user_contractor_id() = p_contractor` is NULL for an unbound caller, so `if not (NULL or false)` = `if NULL` never fired Б├▓ an unbound visitor BYPASSED the gate and could record/revoke any contractor's consent. Fix: `coalesce(Б─╕ = Б─╕, false)`. **Lesson: a `helper() = x` self-check needs coalesce-to-false whenever the helper can return NULL Б─■ 3-valued logic silently opens the gate.** Audited the session's other RPCs: submit_contractor_bank_change + get_my_dc_payments already null-guard explicitly; only the consent pair had it.) Defines what we collect from a DC (operator: DCs are individuals Б─■ ID, background-check consent, bank+book, phone, emergency contact; "think what might happen"; differ by type). Full design spec 131. Also recorded the LINE-OA decision (ADR 0051 addendum): one OA now (staff+DC, per-user menus, audience-gated notifications), client OA later. **Migration A** `20260709000000_contact_doc_types`: ALTER contact_doc_purpose += consent, house_registration, insurance, company_cert, vat_cert, contract (own txn; no pgTAP pin on this enum). **Migration B** `20260709000100_contractor_consents`: contractors += emergency_contact_name/relation/phone + date_of_birth (PII not money Б─■ ride contractors grant/RLS incl. spec-130 own-row read; added to staff column write-grants); `contractor_consent_kind` enum (pdpa_data|background_check); `contractor_consents` table (dated, REVOCABLE Б─■ PDPA; recorded_by, document_idБ├▓signed doc, revoked_at) RLS own-contractor + staff read, RPC-only writes; `record_contractor_consent` (self-for-own OR staff) + `revoke_contractor_consent` (self-for-own OR pm/super) SECURITY DEFINER. **Consent is a first-class record, not a checkbox (PDPA spine).** pgTAP file 51 (15 asserts: catalog/columns/new doc-type cast; record gates self/staff/refused-other; read own/staff/visitor-0; revoke own + revoked_at set + unrelated-party-refused + denied-revoke-intact). **App:** pure `contractorPacketStatus` + `dcTypeOfSubtype` + required-by-type constants (TDD, 8 tests) Б─■ completeness derived, not stored; individual checklist (ID/phone/emergency/bank/bankbook/PDPA+bg-consent) vs company (+reg cert/Ю╦═Ю╦·.20); insurance/house-reg available but NOT required. **No TS hand-extend** this unit Б─■ nothing in TS consumes the new schema yet (helper is self-contained, UI is U2); db:types regenerates post-push, sync guard stays green. U2 = PM + portal UI (emergency-contact + consent capture + doc upload w/ external-write storage RLS + the completeness checklist). Seams: background-check PROVIDER (manual/store-only now), doc expiry reminders.

## Spec 134 U3 - Within-ticket partial delivery via split-on-receipt (2026-06-17)

Status: COMPLETE on prod Б─■ 2026-06-17 (ADR 0052 accepted). Migration `20260714000000_purchase_request_partial_split` merged + `db:push`ed (dry-run clean); `db:test` **60 files / 1280 assertions / 0 failures** (new file 60 = 24); `db:types` regenerated app+worker (commit 7291dd8). The 1Б─⌠2% within-ticket case. **Schema:** `split_from_request_id` lineage column (RPC-only by the column-scoped grant posture, ADR 0038) + `split_purchase_request_on_receipt(p_request_id, p_received_qty, p_received_by?, p_delivery_note?, p_delivered_amount?)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC. Splits an in-transit PO member into a delivered portion (the ORIGINAL, reduced Б─■ sets delivered_at so the existing derive trigger flips it to `delivered` + the audit trigger logs delivery) + a REMAINING child (new row, on_route, same PO, `split_from_request_id`=original, pr_number from the sequence default). Guards: back-office, in-transit member (purchased/on_route), `0<received<ordered`, delivered-amount range. **Amount (ADR 0052 б╖4, operator: proportional default + buyer-editable):** omit `p_delivered_amount` Б├▓ `round(amountц≈received/ordered,2)`; supply Б├▓ buyer value; remainder = original Б┬▓ delivered (family sum = original exactly, per-WP spend preserved). One split audit row (action 'update', ADR 0027/0031 no-new-enum precedent). **UI (U3-ii):** `splitPurchaseRequestOnReceipt` action (relays the RPC) + `PartialReceiveControl` (a "Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╦ Ю╦╡Ю╦┤Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦≥" expander on each in-transit PO-detail line Б─■ qty + editable proportional-prefill amount [back office only] + note); after submit the PO badge becomes `partially_received` via the roll-up (no new derive/display logic Б─■ the split yields ordinary tickets). **Verified-by-checklist** for the UI (auth-gated; the RPC carries the pgTAP). **Spec 134 partial-delivery story (U1 detail б╥ U2 a+b grouping б╥ U3 split б╥ U4a proof) is COMPLETE on prod.** Only U4b (Lalamove auto-POD) remains, blocked on sandbox creds.

## Spec 134 U5 - PO-level receive flow + demote within-ticket partial (2026-06-17)

Status: COMPLETE on prod Б─■ 2026-06-17 (ADR 0053). Migration `20260715000000_receive_po_lines` merged + db:push'd (dry-run clean); db:test **61 files / 1290 / 0** (new file 61 = 10); db:types reconciled (1f50e47). **Reframes the receiving UX to the operator's real delivery distribution** (A ~85% whole PO б╥ B ~14% whole-ticket subset waiting on restock б╥ C ~1% within-ticket made-to-order) Б─■ the photo-per-ticket model made A/B tedious while U3's Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╦ Ю╦╡Ю╦┤Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦≥ was the loud control; now inverted. **Migration:** `receive_po_lines(p_request_ids uuid[], p_received_by?, p_delivery_note?)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC Б─■ back-office gate, in-transit-only (`status in purchased/on_route`), all-or-nothing; sets delivered_at+received_by+delivery_note Б├▓ the existing derive trigger flips status to delivered + the audit trigger logs each line (standard `purchase_request_delivery` rows). No new column; spec-24 photo path + the roll-up unchanged. **UI:** `receivePoLines` action; `PoReceiveSection` (the PO detail's prominent "Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╦┌Ю╦╜Ю╦┤" checklist Б─■ every in-transit line **ticked by default** = Case A one tap; untick the waiting lines = Case B subset, the rest stay on_route Б├▓ PO `partially_received` via roll-up); the within-ticket split (U3) **demoted** to a quiet "Ю╧│Ю╦ Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╦ Ю╦╡Ю╦┤Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦≥" link per line via a new `subtle`/`triggerLabel` prop on `PartialReceiveControl` (Case C). The static "Ю╦ёЮ╦╡Ю╦╒Ю╦│Ю╦╡Ю╦ёЮ╧┐Ю╦≥Ю╧┐Ю╦ Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜" list stays as read-only PO contents. **Delivery cost** ("sometimes paid, sometimes free") deferred to U4b/courier (operator). **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated; RPC carries the pgTAP). **Spec 134 now: U1б╥U2б╥U3б╥U4aб╥U5 on prod; only U4b (Lalamove) parked on creds.**

## Spec 134 U6 - PO progress stepper + delivering (in_transit) roll-up state (2026-06-17)

Status: COMPLETE on prod Б─■ 2026-06-17. **App-only** (pure helper + labels + a presentational component; no schema). typecheck б╥ lint б╥ **969 unit** (+6) б╥ green. Closes two operator-reported gaps on the PO detail: (1) no progress tracker; (2) delivery felt missing Б─■ the PO jumped ordered Б├▓ received because the roll-up folded `on_route` into "ordered". **Roll-up (amends ADR 0044 б╖5):** `PurchaseOrderStatus` gains `in_transit` (Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤); `derivePurchaseOrderStatus` returns it when Б┴╔1 active member is `on_route` and none delivered yet (between `ordered` = all purchased/none shipped, and `partially_received`). Label `Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤` + pill SKY (the per-ticket on_route hue; partially_received also SKY, label disambiguates). **Stepper:** new pure `purchaseOrderStageStates(status)` Б├▓ 3 stages [ordered, in_transit, received] each done/current/pending (+ partial flag on received for partially_received); `PurchaseOrderTracker` (server-safe, mirrors the spec-22 per-ticket tracker geometry) renders Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜ Б├▓ Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤ Б├▓ Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╦┌Ю╦╜Ю╦┤ on the PO detail summary card. So the delivering stage is always visible as a milestone (even when shipment-recording is skipped, ADR 0027) and shows live (sky/Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤) once `record_shipment` fires. TDD: derive on_route cases flipped orderedБ├▓in_transit + stageStates tests first; i18n + status-colors PO_STATES extended. List surfaces (phone PO card, desktop PO header) inherit the new label/pill automatically. **Verified-by-checklist** for the page render (auth-gated; pure helpers carry the tests).

## Spec 135 U4 - Per-delivery proof of delivery (2026-06-17)

Status: COMPLETE on prod Б─■ 2026-06-17 (ADR 0054). Migration `20260721000000_po_attachment_delivery_id` merged + db:push'd (dry-run clean); db:test **63 files / 1331 / 0** (file 50 now 34, +5: delivery_id col + view col + FK violation + back-office insert + view surfaces); db:types reconciled (the two delivery_id FK Relationships entries, app+worker). lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **984 unit** (+5 new TDD) б╥ green. **Closes the spec 135 deliveries arc.** A proof-of-delivery (signed note / received-goods photo) now belongs to the **delivery (Ю╦┤Ю╦╖Ю╦■)** it documents, not the whole PO. **Migration** (mirrors the 20260713000000 purpose migration): `purchase_order_attachments.delivery_id` nullable FK Б├▓ `purchase_order_deliveries(id)` + index + `grant insert(delivery_id)` (ADR 0038 column-scope) + recreate `purchase_order_attachments_current` to carry it. **NO backfill** Б─■ the table is append-only (the block-write trigger rejects UPDATE), so legacy proof (`delivery_id` NULL) surfaces under the PO's **default** (earliest, Ю╦┤Ю╦╖Ю╦■Ю╦≈Ю╦╣Ю╧┬ 1) delivery via the app helper, not a data migration. **App:** `addProofOfDeliveryAttachment` now takes a `deliveryId`, **validated to belong to the PO** (server-side read under RLS) before insert, and stamps it; `ProofOfDeliveryUploader` carries `deliveryId`; pure `groupProofByDelivery(docs, defaultDeliveryId)` (5 unit tests, TDD) maps each doc to its delivery (NULL Б├▓ default); `PoDeliverySection` renders proof **per delivery** Б─■ one block for the 85% single-delivery default (unchanged feel), a per-Ю╦┤Ю╦╖Ю╦■ block (heading "Ю╦┤Ю╦╖Ю╦■Ю╦≈Ю╦╣Ю╧┬ N б╥ Ю╦╚Ю╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦│Ю╦░Ю╦╡Ю╦≥Ю╦│Ю╦╡Ю╦ёЮ╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤" + its own uploader) when the PO is split. Page query adds `delivery_id`, groups, passes `proofByDelivery`. The delivery-belongs-to-PO RLS with-check left as a possible follow-up (action enforces it; the INSERT policy is unchanged, mirroring the purpose migration's minimalism). **Verified-by-checklist** for the UI (auth-gated; helper + pgTAP carry tests). **Spec 135 = U1б╥U2б╥U3б╥U4 on prod;** only U4b (Lalamove auto-POD + per-delivery cost) parked on sandbox creds Б─■ the delivery entity + per-delivery proof/cost are its join point.

Creates a NEW delivery carrying eta/note/cost and repoints the selected lines' `delivery_id`. **Gate:** back office (project_manager/procurement/super_admin) Б─■ **NOT site_admin** (a delivery is procurement's PLAN, not a Ю╦ёЮ╦╠Ю╦ Ю╦┌Ю╦╜Ю╦┤ receive action, U8). **Guards:** every selected id is a distinct in-transit (`purchased`/`on_route`) member of the PO (one count check catches non-member, delivered/rejected/cancelled, and dup ids); no **source delivery emptied** Б─■ each touched delivery keeps Б┴╔1 active line (a delivered line counts, so it keeps a source alive after all its in-transit lines move); cost Б┴╔ 0. ## Spec 137 - Action-state bands + view filter on the site /requests worklist (2026-06-17)

Status: COMPLETE on prod Б─■ 2026-06-17. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **995 unit** (+7 new TDD) б╥ green. **Operator:** site people need more than Ю╦≈Ю╦╠Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦■/Ю╦┌Ю╦╜Ю╦┤Ю╦┴Ю╦╠Ю╦≥, the flat sort "is not intuitive", and "at the very least be able to filter out items received." (I recommended + built; aligns with the locked SA action-state lens, [[worklist-priority-alignment]].) The non-procurement `/requests` view (SA/PM/super) was a flat list (pending by priority, then everything newest-first) + a Ю╦≈Ю╦╠Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦■/Ю╦┌Ю╦╜Ю╦┤Ю╦┴Ю╦╠Ю╦≥ toggle. **Pure helper** `src/lib/purchasing/request-bands.ts` (7 unit tests, TDD): `requestBand(status)` Б├▓ action-state band; `groupRequestsByBand(rows, view)` Б├▓ ordered non-empty bands **Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╦╜Ю╦≥Ю╦╦Ю╦║Ю╦╠Ю╦∙Ю╦╢** (requested) Б├▓ **Ю╦╜Ю╦≥Ю╦╦Ю╦║Ю╦╠Ю╦∙Ю╦╢Ю╧│Ю╦╔Ю╧┴Ю╦╖ Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜** (approved) Б├▓ **Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤** (purchased/on_route) Б├▓ **Ю╧─Ю╦╙Ю╦ёЮ╧┤Ю╦┬Ю╧│Ю╦╔Ю╧┴Ю╦╖** (delivered/site_purchased) Б├▓ **Ю╧└Ю╦║Ю╧┬Ю╦╜Ю╦≥Ю╦╦Ю╦║Ю╦╠Ю╦∙Ю╦╢/Ю╦╒Ю╦│Ю╧─Ю╦╔Ю╦╢Ю╦│** (rejected/cancelled), active bands sorted priority-then-oldest (`comparePendingRequests`), done/closed newest-first; `RequestView` active(default)/done/all with `VIEW_BANDS` Б─■ **active HIDES received+closed** (the operator's minimum). **Page:** `?view=` (default active); the non-procurement filter row is now a **view segmented control** (Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦■Ю╦ЁЮ╧─Ю╦≥Ю╦╢Ю╦≥Ю╦│Ю╦╡Ю╦ё/Ю╧─Ю╦╙Ю╦ёЮ╧┤Ю╦┬Ю╧│Ю╦╔Ю╧┴Ю╦╖/Ю╦≈Ю╦╠Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦■) + a **Ю╧─Ю╦┴Ю╦·Ю╦╡Ю╦╟Ю╦┌Ю╦╜Ю╦┤Ю╦┴Ю╦╠Ю╦≥** toggle (replaces the old Ю╦≈Ю╦╠Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦■/Ю╦┌Ю╦╜Ю╦┤Ю╦┴Ю╦╠Ю╦≥ 2-chip; each preserves the other axis via `reqHref`, defaults omitted from the URL); the list renders as **band sections** (heading + count + cards), 3-way empty state (no requests / none in this view / bands). And the thing site most wants to know Б─■ **is anything late** Б─■ surfaces as a `Ю╧─Ю╦╔Ю╦╒Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╚Ю╦≥Ю╦■ N` danger chip on a band with overdue arrivals (`groupRequestsByBand(rows, view, today)` counts items whose `eta` < today; +3 unit tests, 998 total). ## Spec 95 (hardening) - iOS keyboard-freeze: scroll-independent repaint for short forms (2026-06-17)

Status: code COMPLETE, **NOT device-verified** (desktop preview cannot reproduce the WebKit/iOS-PWA quirk Б─■ operator must confirm on a real iOS PWA, especially a SHORT form). **App-only, no migration.** lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **999 unit** б╥ green. **Operator: "fix the frozen screen after closing the keyboard for good."** Recurrence #2 of the spec-95 blank-after-keyboard glitch (recurrence #1 = the still-focused-field case, fixed 436ee6f). **Root cause:** every `ViewportScrollGuard.repaintScroller` path forced the repaint via `scroller.scrollBy(0,1)` Б─■ which only repaints when `<main>` can actually scroll. A form that fits the viewport (no overflow) can't scroll Б├▓ scrollBy moves nothing Б├▓ the locked scroller (spec 64: body overflow:hidden, `<main>` the only scroller) stays blank. The 85% of long forms recovered; short ones froze "for good". **Fix:** `repaintScroller` now ALSO does a scroll-INDEPENDENT repaint Б─■ a 1px `transform: translateY(1px)` nudge on `<main>`, restored on the next rAF (preserves any existing transform; the 1px shift is invisible for one frame) Б─■ re-rasterizing the layer regardless of content height. Belt-and-suspenders with the existing scroll nudge; both the focusout (force=false, keeps the mid-edit field-to-field skip) and visual-viewport-resize (force=true, the still-focused recurrence) paths get it. TDD: 3rd test in `viewport-scroll-guard.test.tsx` asserts the transform is set inside the repaint and cleared next frame. **Verified-by-checklist** (jsdom has no layout/WebKit; the unit test pins the DOM contract, the real proof is the operator's device test). If it recurs again: next levers are lowering the 80px keyboard-down threshold, nudging on `geometrychange`, or firing across more frames of the ~250ms keyboard slide.

**Recurrence #3 Б─■ "hidden, not frozen" (2026-06-17):** operator reported the prior fix didn't take and reframed the symptom Б─■ the screen feels **hidden** (pushed off), not blank/frozen. That's a DIFFERENT bug than the missing-repaint one. The layout comment (`app/layout.tsx`) says the guard's job is to "snap the locked document back to top Б─╕ (otherwise the header is pushed off)", but `git log -S scrollTo` proves the guard **never** snapped to top Б─■ only the net-zero nudge ever existed, so the header-pushed-off case was unhandled the whole time. Mechanism: body is locked (spec 64 overflow:hidden) so `window`/document scroll should always be 0, but iOS pans the document up to reveal a focused field near the bottom and doesn't always undo that pan on keyboard-close Б├▓ the sticky header sits ABOVE the visible viewport ("hidden"). The net-zero nudge can't fix a real offset. **Fix:** `repaintScroller` now also `window.scrollTo(0, 0)` on keyboard-close (always safe Б─■ a locked body cannot legitimately scroll; does NOT touch `<main>`'s own scroll = the reading position); gated by the same force/mid-edit logic so it never yanks the viewport while the keyboard is still up. TDD: +2 tests (snaps to top on close; does NOT snap while another field is being edited). **1001 unit** б╥ lint б╥ typecheck green. **Still NOT device-verified** Б─■ operator must confirm on a real iOS PWA. If still seen: the pan may be a visual-viewport offset rather than a layout scroll Б├▓ next lever is also zeroing `document.documentElement.scrollTop` / handling `visualViewport.offsetTop`.

**Recurrence #4 Б─■ "BOTTOM BLANK GAP" Б─■ actual root cause (2026-06-17):** prior two fixes (repaint, snap-to-top) didn't take. Diagnostic questions cracked it: operator says a **blank gap at the BOTTOM** (not top, not frozen), recovered by **rotate / navigate / refresh but NOT by scrolling**. That discriminator rules out both earlier hypotheses Б─■ not a paint bug (scrolling would fix it), not a scroll offset (snap-to-top didn't fix it). It's a **stale viewport HEIGHT**: iOS standalone PWA leaves the locked body/`<main>` at the keyboard-REDUCED `100%`/`h-full` height after the keyboard closes, so the vacated bottom strip stays blank; rotate/navigate/refresh fix it because they all force a fresh relayout at the restored height. **Fix:** `repaintScroller` now also pins `document.body.style.height` to the live `window.innerHeight` for one frame, then releases it back to the CSS `h-full` lock on the next rAF Б─■ replicating the rotate relayout so `100%` re-resolves against the correct viewport (own rAF, restores even with no `<main>`). TDD: +1 test (pins to innerHeight, clears next frame). **1002 unit** б╥ lint б╥ typecheck green. The guard now does FOUR things on keyboard-close: height relayout (bottom gap) б╥ window snap-to-top (hidden header) б╥ scroll nudge (blank scrollable) б╥ transform nudge (blank short form). **Still NOT device-verified** Б─■ if the bottom gap persists, escalate from the one-frame toggle to PERMANENT height tracking (set body height = innerHeight on every resize/orientationchange, the `--app-height` pattern) rather than relying on iOS to recompute `100%`.

**Recurrence #5 Б─■ STOP guessing, instrument (2026-06-17):** the height-relayout toggle (#4) also didn't take on device Б─■ operator: "problem still there". Three blind fixes missed because the surface is auth-gated + iOS-PWA-only (no desktop repro), so the actual stale dimension is still unknown. Switched from guessing to MEASURING: new **`ViewportDebug`** flag-gated diagnostic overlay (`src/components/features/chrome/viewport-debug.tsx`, mounted in `app/layout.tsx`) Б─■ renders null unless `?vpdebug=1` (or `localStorage.vpdebug="1"`), otherwise a fixed top-left overlay printing live `innerHeight / visualViewport.height/offsetTop/pageTop / documentElement.clientHeight / body.rectH / main.rectH+clientH+scrollH+scrollTop / window.scrollY / doc.scrollTop / activeElement`, updated on resize/scroll/orientationchange/focusin/focusout (+vv resize/scroll). Operator opens the broken screen with `?vpdebug=1`, closes the keyboard, screenshots the numbers in the blank-gap state Б├▓ tells us which dimension is wrong Б├▓ one definitive fix instead of a 4th guess. TDD: `viewport-debug.test.tsx` (renders null without flag; overlay with flag). **App-only, flag-gated, zero impact on normal use.** lint б╥ typecheck б╥ test green. **TEMPORARY Б─■ remove once the real fix lands.** The viewport-scroll-guard fixes (#2Б─⌠#4) stay in (each is harmless and may help one of the sub-cases); the next fix targets whatever the device numbers reveal.

**REGRESSION + REVERT (2026-06-17):** fixes #2Б─⌠#4 were NOT harmless Б─■ operator: the orange Ю╦√Ю╧┬Ю╦╡Ю╦╒Ю╦ёЮ╦╧Ю╦⌡ hero bar (phase-uploader, `position: fixed inset-x-0 bottom-0`, a descendant of PageShell `<main>`) was "hovering all over the screen". Cause: the #4 `transform: translateY(1px)` nudge on `<main>` Б─■ a CSS transform makes the element the **containing block for its `position:fixed` descendants**, so the fixed capture bar (and any fixed chrome: tab bar, modals, toasts) detaches from the viewport and tracks `<main>`. Worse, the guard's resize path fires `repaintScroller(true)` whenever `innerHeight - vv.height < 80`, which is TRUE even with no keyboard (vv.height Б┴┬ innerHeight), so incidental iOS visualViewport resize/scroll events re-applied the transform constantly Б├▓ the bar wandered. **Action:** reverted `viewport-scroll-guard.tsx` + its test to the last-good pre-regression commit `4b90a3a` (436ee6f baseline = net-zero `scrollBy` nudge only); dropped the transform nudge, the `window.scrollTo(0,0)`, and the body-height pin (all three unverified, all three fired on the always-true gate). **The keyboard bug itself is still UNFIXED** Б─■ but the guard is back to a known-good state and the regression is gone. The `ViewportDebug` overlay (af25bc5/6253d14) stays Б─■ it's a fixed top-left `pointer-events:none` box that transforms no ancestor, so it's safe Б─■ and it's now the path to a real diagnosis. **Lesson:** never put a `transform` on the scroll container Б─■ it reparents all fixed chrome; and the `< 80` resize gate is too loose (fires without a keyboard), so anything behind it must be a true no-op when no keyboard is present.

**Recurrence #7 Б─■ THE FIX (browser-verified) (2026-06-17):** operator sent the actual screenshots. They settled it: post-revert the orange bar is correctly bottom-fixed (regression gone), and the `/requests` create form is **physically clipped at the focused field (Ю╦┬Ю╦ЁЮ╦≥Ю╦╖Ю╦≥/Ю╦╚Ю╦≥Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦╒) with a giant blank gap below** Б─■ the scroller is collapsed to the keyboard-reduced height, not merely unpainted. Confirms the stale-height mechanism: the locked `html Б├▓ body Б├▓ main` chain is all `h-full` (=100%); iOS standalone shrinks the web view for the keyboard and never recomputes `100%` on close, so the root stays short Б├▓ `<main>` clipped Б├▓ blank gap. The #4 one-frame toggle failed because it released back to the broken `100%`. **Fix = new `AppHeightTracker`** (`src/components/features/chrome/app-height-tracker.tsx`, mounted in `app/layout.tsx`): pins `documentElement` + `body` height to the live `window.innerHeight` and re-applies on `resize` / `visualViewport resize` / `orientationchange` / `pageshow` / `focusout`(+100ms settle), so the keyboard-close resize restores the full height for real instead of relying on iOS to recompute `100%`. `<main>`'s `h-full` follows the corrected root. **No transform** (the regression lesson) Б─■ only an explicit root height. **Browser-VERIFIED in the preview** (the first fix in this arc confirmed before shipping): at 812 the tracker pins html/body/main = 812px; shrink the viewport to 500 + fire resize Б├▓ all track to 500; restore to 812 + fire resize Б├▓ all restore to 812 (the keyboard openБ├▓close cycle); zero console errors. TDD: `app-height-tracker.test.tsx` (pins on mount; re-applies the restored height on resize). lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1002 unit** (147 files) green. **Still owed: operator device confirmation** on the real iOS PWA (the in-app keyboard fires the resize/visualViewport events the preview can't), but the mechanism is now proven, not guessed. `ViewportDebug` overlay stays until confirmed, then both it and any vestigial guard nudge can be removed.

**Recurrence #8 Б─■ wrong API found by research; corrected to visualViewport (2026-06-17):** #7 didn't work either, and web research (martijnhols.nl OSK article, htmhell viewport guide, quirksmode) explained why: **on iOS the soft keyboard is a SEPARATE LAYER Б─■ the layout viewport never changes, so `window.innerHeight` stays constant and the window `resize` event does NOT fire when the keyboard opens/closes.** #7's `AppHeightTracker` was built on innerHeight + window resize, so it literally could not respond to the keyboard. Also confirmed: `interactive-widget=resizes-content` is NOT implemented in iOS Safari, so the declarative fix is out. **The only reliable signal is `window.visualViewport`** (`.height` shrinks; the `resize`/`scroll` events fire). **Rewrote `AppHeightTracker`** to publish `Math.round(visualViewport.height)` as the **`--app-vh`** CSS variable on `documentElement`, driven by `visualViewport.resize`/`scroll` (+ window resize/orientationchange/pageshow + focusout fallbacks + a 300ms delayed re-read for iOS's close-lag where visualViewport.height doesn't settle immediately). **PageShell's `<main>`** is now `style={{ height: "var(--app-vh, 100%)" }}` (h-full class stays as the pre-JS/non-iOS fallback) Б─■ so the scroller tracks the actually-visible area: it shrinks above the keyboard and restores to full on close. CSS variable only Б─■ **NO transform** (the reverted regression) and no scroll change, so fixed chrome is untouched. **Browser-VERIFIED in the preview:** at 812 Б├▓ `--app-vh` 812px, main computed 812px; shrink the visual viewport to 500 Б├▓ main 500 (the `visualViewport.resize` listener fires automatically, unlike window resize); restore to 812 Б├▓ main 812; zero console errors. TDD: `app-height-tracker.test.tsx` rewritten with a mocked `window.visualViewport` (publishes --app-vh on mount; restores on visualViewport resize). lint б╥ typecheck б╥ test green. **Device pass still owed** Б─■ the preview proves the wiring + the right API, but only the real iOS keyboard fires the genuine visualViewport events. If it STILL fails, enable `ViewportDebug` (cornerц≈5 / `?vpdebug=1`) and screenshot Б─■ the live vv.height vs innerHeight numbers will confirm the model.

**Recurrence #9 Б─■ THE ACTUAL CAUSE, from on-device numbers (2026-06-17).** Made `ViewportDebug` ON by default (#8.5) so the next screenshot carried the metrics. It did, and it ended six rounds of guessing. **Broken state, keyboard CLOSED (`active=body`): `window.scrollY = 389`, `document.documentElement.scrollTop = 389`** (also `vv.height=744`, `vv.offsetTop=49`, `doc.clientH=793`). The body is LOCKED (spec 64 overflow:hidden) so the document must always be at scroll 0 Б─■ it was at **389**. iOS scrolls the documentElement to reveal the focused input when the keyboard opens and **does not reset it on close**, leaving the whole page shifted up ~389px = exactly the bottom blank gap. **Not paint, not main-height, not a stale 100% Б─■ a stuck DOCUMENT scroll.** Every prior fix was the wrong axis; the `--app-vh`/visualViewport-height experiment (#8) even made `<main>` 49px short (744 vs the 793 layout) and is now REVERTED. **Fix:** `ViewportScrollGuard` rewritten to force `documentElement.scrollTop` / `body.scrollTop` / `window.scrollTo(0,0)` back to 0 when the keyboard is DOWN (`innerHeight - visualViewport.height < 100`, so it never fights iOS revealing the input mid-edit), fired on focusout + visualViewport resize/scroll + orientationchange/pageshow, with 300ms/600ms re-reads for iOS's late settle. Only the document scroll is touched Б─■ `<main>`'s reading scroll is left alone; no transform, no height changes. Reverted: deleted `AppHeightTracker` + its test, removed it from layout, PageShell `<main>` back to plain `h-full`. TDD: guard test rewritten (resets doc scroll to 0 when keyboard down; does NOT reset when keyboard up). lint б╥ typecheck б╥ test green; preview confirms no regression (main full height, no console errors). `ViewportDebug` stays default-on for the confirmation screenshot Б─■ expectation: in the broken-flow re-test, `window.scrollY`/`doc.scrollTop` now read 0. Remove the overlay once the operator confirms.

**Recurrence #10 Б─■ THE REAL ROOT: iOS auto-zoom on input focus (2026-06-17).** After the doc-scroll-reset, operator: **"zooming out to 100% solves the blank portion."** That reframes it Б─■ the page was ZOOMED IN, and the `scrollY=389` pan was the zoom-pan, not an independent document scroll. Cause confirmed in code: the form fields are NOT the `ui/input` primitive (which is `text-base`=16px on mobile) Б─■ they're hand-rolled `<input>`/`<select>`/`type=date`/`<textarea>` at **`text-sm` = 14px** (`purchase-request-form.tsx` lines 201/222/241/297/308/358, and the same pattern across other forms). **iOS auto-zooms into any focused input whose font-size < 16px**, and a standalone PWA leaves the page zoomed + panned after blur Б├▓ the blank portion; manual zoom-to-100% clears it. **Fix (design-preserving, global):** viewport meta now `width=device-width, initial-scale=1, maximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no` (Next `viewport` export: `maximumScale:1, userScalable:false`) Б─■ a standalone PWA honors it and iOS no longer auto-zooms on focus, so the field-first `text-sm` sizes stay unchanged. **Trade-off:** disables pinch-zoom app-wide (acceptable for a native-feel ops PWA; operator framed zoom as the bug). Alternative if pinch-zoom must stay: bump every form input to 16px (enlarges field text, many files) Б─■ offered to operator. Verified in preview: the rendered `<meta name=viewport>` content = `Б─╕maximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no`; no console errors. Added `vv.scale` to `ViewportDebug` so the operator can confirm scale stays 1.00. The doc-scroll-reset (#9) stays as defense. lint б╥ typecheck б╥ test green.

## Spec 95 Б─■ RESOLVED + cleanup (2026-06-18)

Operator confirmed on device: **no more zoom, no blank portion.** Root cause = iOS auto-zoom on `<16px` form inputs; fix = `maximum-scale=1` in the root `viewport` export (global Б─■ the only `viewport` export in the app, so it covers every form on every screen). **Cleanup refactor:** removed the temporary `ViewportDebug` overlay (component + test + layout mount + corner-tap gesture); confirmed no dangling `--app-vh` / `AppHeightTracker` / `vpdebug` references remain. **Kept** `ViewportScrollGuard`, reframed as defense-in-depth for the spec-64 body-lock invariant (document scroll stays 0 if iOS scrolls the documentElement to reveal a focused input) Б─■ a cheap no-op in the normal case; its header comment now points at `maximum-scale=1` as the primary fix. Browser-verified: overlay gone, viewport meta still `Б─╕maximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no`, no `--app-vh` leftover, no console errors. lint б╥ typecheck б╥ test green. The spec-95 saga (#1Б─⌠#10) is closed; memory `ios-keyboard-repaint-freeze` rewritten to lead with the auto-zoom root cause + the process lesson (for device-only bugs: ship a metrics overlay first, get one screenshot, then fix the named dimension). **Possible follow-up (not done, scope):** the 14px hand-rolled inputs duplicate styling across forms Б─■ a shared form-field input component would centralize the size decision and document the <16px-zoom trap.

## Spec 138 U1 Б─■ Ю╦∙Ю╧┴Ю╦╜Ю╦┤Ю╦∙Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╦∙Ю╦╡Ю╦║Ю╦■Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦≥ urgent-follow-up panel (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE Б─■ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1003 unit** (+4 new TDD) б╥ green. **Source:** a Claude Design (claude.ai/design) handoff bundle ("Mobile-first redesign for tablets", primary file `PRC Ops Worklist Mobile.dc.html`) Б─■ the operator mocked the desktopБ├▓mobile worklist UX and asked to implement the relevant aspects.
