Field-First tokens only (danger trio + ink/edge/card) Б─■ passes design-doctrine (no green-\*, no min-h-9). **Page** (`src/app/requests/page.tsx`): computes `attentionItems` for procurement after the existing `amountById` admin read (the panel shows amount Б─■ already back-office for procurement; no new query, no new money exposure), renders the panel in the procurement column right after the KPI grid, before the filters, only when non-empty; the footer href reuses `buildWorklistQuery({ ...filter, overdue: true })` (same target as the Ю╧─Ю╦│Ю╦╢Ю╦≥Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╚Ю╦≥Ю╦■ tile). Named distinct from the existing `AttentionCard` callout primitive (different thing). **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated procurement page Б├▓ no preview; the pure helper carries correctness). Spec doc `138-mobile-worklist-redesign.md` (index updated; also backfilled the missing 136/137 index rows). **Next units (not started, one-per-session):** U2 KPI hero restyle (amber-gradient Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜ tile + icons + tap-to-filter); U3 scrollable status-chip filter with live counts (replace the status `<select>`). **Refinement (2026-06-18, operator: "Remove Ю╦∙Ю╧┴Ю╦╜Ю╦┤Ю╦∙Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╦∙Ю╦╡Ю╦║Ю╦■Ю╧┬Ю╦╖Ю╦≥ section from phone view"):** wrapped the render in `hidden lg:block` so the panel now shows only on tablet/desktop (lg+) Б─■ its origin in the design (the desktop `.dc.html` added it first, mobile mirrored). On the phone the Ю╧─Ю╦│Ю╦╢Ю╦≥Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╚Ю╦≥Ю╦■ KPI tile (its filter toggle) stays the chase entry point; the panel read as redundant there. className-only, no logic/helper/test change; lint б╥ typecheck б╥ test green.

## Spec 138 U2 Б─■ desktop KPI hero row (2026-06-18)

## Spec 138 U3 Б─■ scrollable status-chip filter with live counts (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE Б─■ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1015 unit** (+8 new TDD: 5 chip helper + 3 band axis) б╥ green. **U3 = the desktop/mobile mock's status chips.** Replaces the procurement worklist status `<select>` with a horizontally-scrollable row of BAND pills (Ю╦≈Ю╦╠Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╚Ю╦║Ю╦■ / Ю╦╜Ю╦≥Ю╦╦Ю╦║Ю╦╠Ю╦∙Ю╦╢Ю╧│Ю╦╔Ю╧┴Ю╦╖=`to_order` / Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤=`in_transit` / Ю╧─Ю╦│Ю╦╢Ю╦≥Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╚Ю╦≥Ю╦■=overdue), each with a LIVE count. **Introduces the band filter axis** the U2 seam flagged Б─■ a single raw `status` enum can't express the in_transit band's purchased-OR-on_route set, so a later unit can now make the Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜/Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤ KPI tiles tap-to-filter (reuse this axis). **Filter axis** (`src/lib/purchasing/worklist-filter.ts`): `ProcurementFilter` += `band: ProcurementBand | null`; `matchesProcurementFilter` AND-composes it (`procurementBand(row.status) === filter.band`); `buildWorklistQuery` serializes `?band=to_order|in_transit` (between project + status). The raw `status` axis STAYS (no UI now, but `?status=rejected` still surfaces the banded-out rejected/cancelled history Б─■ the only escape, kept to avoid a regression). **Pure helper** `src/lib/purchasing/worklist-status-chips.ts` `buildWorklistStatusChips({rows, filter, todayIso})` Б├▓ 4 chip descriptors `{key,label,count,href,active}` in order (allб╥to_orderб╥in_transitб╥overdue); counts reuse the spec-105 `procurementSummary` (so they agree with the KPI hero) + `all` = rows with a non-null band; `rows` is the supplier/project-narrowed set Б├▓ counts are LIVE to those axes; each `href` reuses `buildWorklistQuery` preserving supplier/project/status while setting band+overdue per chip; `active` = overdue wins, else band, else all (5 unit tests, TDD). **Component** `WorklistStatusChips` (server-safe, presentational, no `'use client'`): `overflow-x-auto` `<Link>` pill row, each label + count badge, active pill `bg-fill/text-on-fill` Б─■ mirrors the spec-137 `worklistChipClass`, min-h-11 tap floor, Field-First tokens only (passes design-doctrine: no green-\*/no-min-h-9). **Page** (`src/app/requests/page.tsx`): parses `?band` (validated against `PROCUREMENT_BANDS`), builds the chips over supplier/project-narrowed rows, renders `<WorklistStatusChips>` between the KPI grid and the supplier/project pickers; `filterActive` += `filter.band`. Band filtering flows through `matchesProcurementFilter` + the existing `groupByProcurementBand` (an active band yields that one group); the `status` flat-group branch is untouched. **`ProcurementFilters`**: removed the status `<select>` (+ its now-dead `STATUS_OPTIONS` / label import / `PurchaseRequestStatus` type); supplier/project pickers stay; the Ю╦╔Ю╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦┤Ю╦∙Ю╦╠Ю╦╖Ю╦│Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╦┤ clear-all now also resets `band`. **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated procurement page Б├▓ no preview; pure helpers carry correctness; operator device/desktop look-feedback is acceptance). Spec doc updated (U3 Change section). **Open question (decided):** removing the `<select>` drops the only VISIBLE path to filter rejected/cancelled Б─■ kept reachable via the `?status=` URL but no longer a control (spec-sanctioned; bands already drop those from the pipeline). **Spec 138 = U1б╥U2б╥U3 done.** Next possible unit: make the Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜/Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤ KPI tiles tap-to-filter (the band axis is now in place); sortable grid columns (care: overrides priority/PO-contiguity order).

## Spec 138 U4 Б─■ KPI hero tiles tap-to-filter (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE Б─■ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1019 unit** (+4 net: the `worklist-kpis` test rewrote from 4 Б├▓ 8 cases) б╥ green. U4 = the final mock affordance: the Ю╦ёЮ╦╜Ю╦╙Ю╦╠Ю╧┬Ю╦┤Ю╦▀Ю╦╥Ю╧┴Ю╦╜ (`to_order`) and Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╔Ю╦╠Ю╦┤Ю╦┬Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╙Ю╧┬Ю╦┤ (`in_transit`) KPI hero tiles are now clickable band toggles (deferred from U2 "needs the bandБ├▓status mapping", which U3 then built), reusing the U3 band axis. **Pure helper** (`src/lib/purchasing/worklist-kpis.ts`): `buildWorklistKpis` now takes `{ summary, outstanding, filter }` (dropped the pre-built `overdueHref`/`overdueActive` pair) and derives every tile's `href`/`active` internally via `buildWorklistQuery` Б─■ mirroring the U3 `buildWorklistStatusChips` so the toggle logic lives in one place. The Ю╧─Ю╦│Ю╦╢Ю╦≥Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╚Ю╦≥Ю╦■ tile is UNCHANGED Б─■ exactly the existing chase toggle `buildWorklistQuery({ ...filter, overdue: !filter.overdue })` / `active = filter.overdue` / danger-when-`overdue > 0 || filter.overdue`; Ю╦└Ю╧┴Ю╦╡Ю╦┤Ю╦┬Ю╧┬Ю╦╡Ю╦╒ stays static (`href: null`). **`WorklistKpiTile`: no change** Б─■ its `href`Б├▓`<Link>`+pressed-ring branch (U2 built it for the Ю╧─Ю╦│Ю╦╢Ю╦≥Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╚Ю╦≥Ю╦■ tile) already covers the two new band tiles; the hot/shipping tones flow through it unchanged. **Page** (`src/app/requests/page.tsx`): passes `filter` to `buildWorklistKpis` (dropped the inline `overdueHref`/`overdueActive` args; `buildWorklistQuery` import stays Б─■ the U1 panel footer still uses it); updated the stale "only the Ю╧─Ю╦│Ю╦╢Ю╦≥Ю╦│Ю╦ЁЮ╦╚Ю╦≥Ю╦■ tile is a filter toggle" comment to note all three pipeline tiles toggle. 8 unit tests (TDD): order/captions, static tones, band-tile href+idle, active band toggles off, band hrefs preserve supplier/project + clear overdue, overdue chase toggle preserved, outstanding static, overdue tone. **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated procurement page Б├▓ no preview; the pure helper carries correctness; operator device/desktop look-feedback is acceptance). ## Spec 139 U1 Б─■ App-feel slice 3: optimistic worker active-toggle (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE Б─■ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1021 unit** (+2 new TDD) б╥ green. App-feel slice 3 (optimistic UI) was the last deferred slice Б─■ done CAREFULLY per-surface, payroll-safe only. U1 = the worker active-toggle on `/workers` (`WorkerRow` in `src/components/features/labor/worker-roster-manager.tsx`), the clean safe pick: already a client component, the toggle reads `worker.active` only for presentation (name colour, `(Ю╦⌡Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╧┐Ю╦┼Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥)` suffix, button label), nothing server-computed beside it. **Introduces React 19 `useOptimistic`** (was zero usage in the codebase). **Change:** replaced the toggle's `busy` + success-only `router.refresh()` with `committedActive = useState(worker.active)` (post-mount truth, advanced only by a successful flip) + `optimisticActive = useOptimistic(committedActive, (_, next) => next)` + `useTransition` (`isToggling`). `toggleActive` is now sync: inside `startToggle(async Б─╕)` it `setOptimisticActive(next)` (instant flip), awaits `updateWorker({ id, active: next })`, and on ok `setCommittedActive(next)` (commit Б─■ the optimistic falls through to it when the transition ends, **no `router.refresh`** Б├▓ the flicker is gone), on `!ok` `toast.error(result.error)` (the optimistic auto-reverts to `committedActive` = the rollback, now explained via the slice-1 toast channel Б─■ the toggle previously failed **silently**). The row renders name colour / `(Ю╦⌡Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╧┐Ю╦┼Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥)` suffix / button label from `optimisticActive`; button `disabled={isToggling}` (no double-fire race). **Untouched** (out of scope): the add-worker form + per-row edit-save stay pessimistic (they surface server validation + need the new/edited row to appear Б├▓ keep `router.refresh`; `useRouter` import stays); the action + RPC + page unchanged; no styling/class change (design-doctrine green). **Tests** (`tests/unit/worker-roster-manager.test.tsx`, +2): optimistic flip-before-server + commit (deferred-promise: label flips to Ю╧─Ю╦⌡Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╧┐Ю╦┼Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥ + `(Ю╦⌡Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╧┐Ю╦┼Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥)` suffix appears while pending, `updateWorker({id:"w1",active:false})`, **no `router.refresh`**; resolve ok Б├▓ stays flipped); rollback + toast (`{ok:false}` Б├▓ reverts to Ю╦⌡Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╧┐Ю╦┼Ю╧┴Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥, suffix gone, `toast.error` fired, no refresh). The 4 existing notes/picker tests unchanged. **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated pm/super `/workers` Б├▓ no preview; the component tests carry correctness; operator on-device eyeball = acceptance, the slice-76/77/78 convention). Spec doc `139-app-feel-optimistic-ui.md` written (index row added; spec-138 index row relabelled to the full mock). **Next:** more payroll-safe optimistic surfaces (later units, per-surface); slice 5 motion (CSS list-enter via `@starting-style`; route View Transitions = guarded spike only). **Care recorded:** money/payment + labor-day logging surfaces are explicitly NOT optimistic candidates (server-computed / auditable).

## Spec 140 U1 Б─■ App-feel slice 5: staggered list-enter motion (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE Б─■ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1025 unit** (+4 new TDD) б╥ **build green** (CSS compiles Б─■ ran `pnpm build` since CI/eslint don't cover globals.css). Pivoted to slice 5 (motion) after an investigation showed slice-3's remaining optimistic surfaces all carry desync (WP hold-status is a central field read across the page) or sensitivity (bank-change approval, consent) risk Б─■ the worker toggle was the one uniquely-clean surface (operator chose the pivot). Slice 5 U1 = the **safe half** only: a CSS-driven, reduced-motion-gated staggered list-enter on the WP worklist (the most-opened screen). Route View Transitions stay a guarded spike (out of scope). **Pure helper** `src/lib/ui/list-enter.ts` `listEnterProps(index)` Б├▓ `{ className:"list-enter", style:{"--enter-index": step} }` where `step = clamp(trunc(index), 0, LIST_ENTER_STAGGER_CAP=8)` Б─■ the cap is load-bearing (a long list's tail must not wait seconds; rows past the cap share the last step), the testable seam (4 tests: index, clamp-0/negative, cap-tail, trunc-fraction, TDD). **`globals.css`** `@keyframes list-enter` (opacity 0Б├▓1, translateY 6pxБ├▓0) + `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: no-preference){ .list-enter{ animation: list-enter 240ms ease-out both; animation-delay: calc(var(--enter-index,0) * 35ms) } }` Б─■ matches the spec-76 `toast-in` / spec-78 `sheet-up` pattern; `both` holds the row invisible through its stagger then settles visible; reduced-motion users get static fully-visible rows (the `from{opacity:0}` only applies while the animation is attached, which only happens inside the no-preference query Б├▓ no FOUC). **`WorklistRow`** gained optional `enterIndex?: number` (merged into the root `<Link>` Б─■ appends the class + sets the style var; omitted Б├▓ every existing caller untouched). **`work-package-list.tsx`** passes `enterIndex={i}` from the map index at the 3 WorklistRow render sites (grouped-by-band / flat action-state / deliverable-group `<li>`) so the WP list glides in uniformly in every group mode. Server-safe (no `'use client'`; class+style are plain markup), zero data risk. **Verified-by-checklist + build** (auth-gated project page Б├▓ no preview; the helper test carries the cap logic; CSS animation isn't unit-testable Б├▓ operator on-device eyeball = acceptance, the slice-77 visual-slice precedent; design-doctrine green Б─■ "list-enter" trips no green-\*/min-h-9 rule). Spec doc `140-app-feel-motion.md` written (index row added). **Next:** more lists (procurement worklist cards, contacts, suppliers, requests Б─■ fast-follows reusing `listEnterProps`); route / View Transitions later (guarded spike, never the foundation); slice 3 optimistic continues per-surface (payroll-safe only).

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-18.** lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1086 unit** б╥ green; **pgTAP file 70 green post-push (30/30; full suite 70 files / 1455 asserts, 0 failures)**; `db:push` applied `20260728000000`; `db:types` reconciled. Prod data is tiny (2 projects, 2 PMs, 3 site_admins; backfill enrolled the 1 lead) + super_admin sees all, so add the right people to each project via project settings (spec 80 UI). **Verified-by-checklist** (RLS is the SUT; pgTAP 70 + the regression suite carry correctness; operator on-device pass = acceptance). **Next:** U2 Б─■ enable `project_coordinator` as a real role (roleHome Б├▓ `/projects` + add to PROJECT_VIEW_ROLES so the see-all coordinator can actually browse; currently lands on /coming-soon). ## Spec 142 U7 Б─■ import work packages from CSV (paste) (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-18.** App-only, **no migration** (reuses the wp-import parser + U4's create_work_package RPC). lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1094 unit (160 files; +3 TDD: import-work-packages-sheet)** б╥ green. Surfaces the CLI-only `pnpm import:wp` flow in-app for the non-dev operator. PM/super get a **Ю╦≥Ю╦ЁЮ╧─Ю╦┌Ю╧┴Ю╦╡ CSV** button Б├▓ paste rows (`code,name,description` with header) Б├▓ valid rows created. **Chose paste-textarea over file upload** Б─■ robust + testable (jsdom File.text() is flaky) + mobile-friendly (operator is on mobile). **Action** `importWorkPackagesCsv(projectId, csvText)`: PM_ROLES gate Б├▓ fetch existing codes (RLS read; PM is a member) Б├▓ `parseAndValidate(csv, existingCodes)` (ADR 0014 parser Б─■ header-based, dup-in-file + already-exists + blank checks) Б├▓ on parser errors return first 8 joined (textarea lets fix+retry) Б├▓ else create each valid row via `create_work_package` **sequentially** (definer RPC sidesteps the work_packages table-grant; sequential so a mid-batch failure reports how far it got) Б├▓ `{ok, inserted}`. **UI:** `ImportWorkPackagesSheet` (BottomSheet + monospace textarea + multi-line `whitespace-pre-line` error alert + router.refresh). Page wiring: added to the PM-only WP-heading button group (now `Ю╦≥Ю╦ЁЮ╧─Ю╦┌Ю╧┴Ю╦╡ CSV` б╥ `Ю╦└Ю╦╠Ю╦■Ю╦╔Ю╦╜Ю╦│Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥` б╥ `+ Ю╧─Ю╦·Ю╦╢Ю╧┬Ю╦║Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥`, flex-wrap). **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated page Б├▓ /login in preview; 3 component tests cover submit-gate/success-refresh/error; the parser has its own unit suite; create_work_package green in pgTAP 69; operator on-device = acceptance). Spec 142 doc gains U7. **Seam:** per-row RPC (fine for onboarding-sized CSVs; a bulk RPC is a later optimization if imports get large). **Onboarding WP-seeding now: manual (U4) б╥ copy-from-project (U6) б╥ CSV (U7) all shipped.** **Next / last:** U5 Б─■ WP template by project_type (`wp_templates` table + `apply_wp_template` RPC + a starter seed the operator edits).

## Spec 143 U3 Б─■ complete the membership-scoping U1 missed (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-18.** lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1096 unit** б╥ green; **full pgTAP suite 73 files / 1489 asserts, 0 failures** post-push; `db:push` applied `20260731000000` + `20260732000000` (fix-forward, below); `db:types` reconciled. A **full-project-lifecycle audit** (4 parallel explorers) found U1's "full isolation" was incomplete: three project-scoped child tables still had role-level SELECT (cross-project leak to PM/site_admin), and the SELECT-only U1 left the app write policies role-level (a non-member could write a row for a project they can't read). **Migration `20260731000000`:** scoped `labor_logs` (staff SELECT only Б─■ the bound-contractor self-read untouched) + `work_package_dependencies` SELECT via `can_see_wp`; mirrored the membership gate onto the **8 app write policies** (photo_logs INSERT, approvals INSERT, purchase_requests app-INSERT, deliverables INSERT+UPDATE, reports INSERT, work_packages UPDATE Б─■ each KEEPS its role list so `project_coordinator` stays read-only; `labor_logs`/`wp_dependencies` are RPC-write-only so no write policy to mirror). Authoritative current policies pulled from `pg_policies` first (not stale files). **Self-inflicted regression + fix-forward:** `20260731000000` also tried to scope `photo_markups` (SELECTБ├▓`can_see_photo_log`, + helper). `photo_markups`' INSERT policy self-references `photo_markups` (tombstone-target EXISTS) Б─■ safe only under a trivial role SELECT policy; under a function SELECT policy Postgres raised **42P17 infinite recursion** on every markup INSERT (caught by pgTAP files 31 + the test, but the migration was already pushed Б├▓ prod markup-insert briefly broken). **`20260732000000`** reverts `photo_markups` to its original working policies + drops the unused `can_see_photo_log` Б─■ prod un-broken. **pgTAP file 73** (plan 12): labor_logs + wp_dependencies + 7 write-mirror wirings + wp_dependencies end-to-end (member sees dep / non-member doesn't). **Two existing suites repaired:** `29-labor-capture` got a membership seed (its `correct_labor_log` id-lookup reads labor_logs as the PM Б─■ now scoped); `31-photo-markups` returns to green once `photo_markups` reverted. **Verified-by-checklist** (RLS is the SUT; pgTAP 73 + the suite carry it). **Lesson:** scoping a SELECT policy on a table whose own write policy self-joins that table triggers 42P17 (ADR 0011 trap) Б─■ needs a SECURITY DEFINER tombstone-target helper (pr_attachment_tombstone_target_ok precedent). **Remaining leak (documented, deferred to U4):** `photo_markups` is still role-level (low sensitivity Б─■ drawing annotations). `labor_logs` (the sensitive one Б─■ worker/day data) IS closed. **SPEC 143 now: U1 (RLS) + U2 (coordinator) + U3 (labor_logs/wp_dependencies + write-mirror) on prod; U4 (photo_markups via definer helper) is the one open item.**

## Spec 143 U4 Б─■ scope photo_markups (recursion-free) (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-18. SPEC 143 COMPLETE.** lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1096 unit** б╥ green; **full pgTAP suite 74 files / 1501 asserts, 0 failures** post-push; `db:push` applied `20260733000000`; `db:types` reconciled. Closes the last read-leak the lifecycle audit found Б─■ `photo_markups` was still role-level (cross-project). **Migration `20260733000000`:** recreates `can_see_photo_log(uuid)` (dropped in U3's revert) + adds `photo_markup_tombstone_target_ok(uuid,uuid)` Б─■ a SECURITY DEFINER helper that performs the tombstone-target self-read (bypassing RLS, `auth.uid()` still the caller so the creator-pin holds). `photo_markups` SELECT Б├▓ `can_see_photo_log`; INSERT keeps the content/own-tombstone rule but the tombstone branch now calls the helper instead of an inline `EXISTS (select Б─╕ from photo_markups Б─╕)`, so the policy no longer self-joins the table Б├▓ **no 42P17** (the U3 failure mode). Role list kept (coordinator read-only). **pgTAP file 74** (plan 12): both helpers exist + secdef, SELECT/INSERT wiring, and behaviourally the **exact content+tombstone INSERT that recursed in U3 now `lives_ok`** for a member, non-member sees 0 + INSERT denied, visitor sees 0. **Existing `31-photo-markups` (the comprehensive markup insert/tombstone/current-view suite) passes under the scoped policies** (its users are members via the U1 seed) Б─■ strong real-world coverage that the recursion is gone and the member path is intact. **Lesson applied:** the pr_attachment_tombstone_target_ok pattern (definer helper for a self-referential append-only policy) is the canonical fix whenever such a table gets a function-based SELECT policy. **ADR 0056 "full isolation" is now actually complete** across all project-scoped tables (projects, work_packages, deliverables, photo_logs, approvals, purchase_requests, reports, labor_logs, work_package_dependencies, photo_markups); the only remaining write-side note is the labor RPCs (log_labor_day/correct_labor_log) gate on role + WP-status but not membership Б─■ residual defense-in-depth (UI is read-locked for non-members), recorded, not exploitable.

## Spec 144 U1 Б─■ defect rework: 'rework' status + reopen RPC (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-18.** lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1097 unit (+1: rework transition assert)** б╥ green; **full pgTAP suite 75 files / 1511 asserts, 0 failures** post-push; `db:push` applied `20260734000000` (enum) + `20260734000100` (RPC); `db:types` reconciled. Closes the lifecycle-audit gap "complete is terminal" Б─■ operator: "complete doesn't mean defect-free." **Model (operator-chosen):** reopen to a new `rework` WP status (not reuse in_progress, not a punch-list entity); `complete Б├▓ rework Б├▓ re-capture After Б├▓ pending_approval Б├▓ complete`. **Reportable by site_admin + PM/super** (field finds defects; PM re-approves). **Migrations:** `rework` added to `work_package_status` in its OWN migration (PG: can't use a new enum value in the tx that adds it; `add value if not exists`), then `reopen_work_package_for_defect(p_wp,p_reason)` Б─■ SECURITY DEFINER, role-gated (sa/pm/super) + membership-gated (`can_see_wp`, ADR 0056), complete-only, flips to `rework` + writes an `audit_log` row (`action='other'`, payload `{event:'wp_reopened_for_defect',reason}`, actor captured); non-complete/empty-reasonБ├▓22023, wrong-role/non-memberБ├▓42501. **Transition wiring:** `TRANSITIONABLE_FROM_STATUSES` += `rework` (after-photo from rework Б├▓ pending_approval); labor already allowed in rework (log_labor_day blocks only complete); list-filter "outstanding" shows rework automatically; cost re-freezes on re-approve (existing path). **Enum-add ripple Б─■ all consumers handled, typecheck-surfaced (the safety net):** `WORK_PACKAGE_STATUS_LABEL` (Ю╦┤Ю╦╡Ю╦≥Ю╧│Ю╦│Ю╧┴Ю╧└Ю╦┌), `workPackageStatusPillClasses` (amber), `deriveActionBand` (reworkБ├▓todo) + `nextAction` (capture), `schedule-gantt` `STATUS_STYLE` (amber, pct 90; this one was caught only by typecheck Б─■ a Record the grep would've missed). **pgTAP file 75** (plan 10) + enum pin (file 08) Б├▓ six values. **Verified-by-checklist** (pure transition predicate unit-tested; RPC pgTAP'd; UI is U2). **Next:** U2 Б─■ the "report defect" control on the WP page (complete-only, SA/PM/super) Б├▓ reopen + show the rework status + reason from the latest audit row.

## Spec 145 Б─■ lock new work on a completed project (warranty-aware) (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod Б─■ 2026-06-18.** lint б╥ typecheck б╥ **1100 unit** б╥ green; **full pgTAP suite 76 files / 1521 asserts, 0 failures** post-push; `db:push` applied `20260735000000`; `db:types` reconciled. Operator decision: a project locks once completed Б─■ **caveat:** completion Б┴═ full closure (client retains a warranty %, Buildall 5% for a year; defects surface in that window), so the lock blocks NEW work but must NOT block warranty defect-rework. **Enforcement = a `BEFORE INSERT` trigger on `work_packages`** (`work_packages_block_insert_on_closed_project`, raises `P0002`) gated by `project_is_open(uuid)` (status in active/on_hold) Б─■ **one chokepoint** over every WP-creation path (manual/template/copy/CSV) without re-typing the 3 creation RPCs, and **INSERT-only** so spec-144 reopen-to-rework (an UPDATE) + the rework WP's capture/labor/approval cycle keep working on a completed project (the warranty carve-out falls out for free; gates on WP status, not project status). The **project record stays editable** (status Б├▓ active to reopen the project; record retention notes in settings). **Actions** map `P0002` Б├▓ "Ю╧┌Ю╦└Ю╦ёЮ╦┤Ю╦│Ю╦╡Ю╦ёЮ╦≥Ю╦╣Ю╧┴Ю╦⌡Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╧│Ю╦╔Ю╧┴Ю╦╖ Ю╧─Ю╦⌡Ю╦╢Ю╦■Ю╧┌Ю╦└Ю╦ёЮ╦┤Ю╦│Ю╦╡Ю╦ёЮ╦│Ю╧┬Ю╦╜Ю╦≥Б─╕" (createWorkPackage/copyWorkPackages/applyWpTemplate/importWorkPackagesCsv). **UI (project page):** added `status` to the project select + `projectOpen`; when closed, hides the seeding controls + onboarding checklist and shows a lock banner pointing to settings. **pgTAP file 76** (plan 11): helper truth table, direct-insert + all 3 RPCs blocked on a completed project (P0002), create still works on active, **reopen-for-defect still works on a completed project (warranty)**; fixtures seed WPs while active then flip to completed (so the seed doesn't trip the trigger). **Verified-by-checklist** (DB lock pgTAP'd; UI gate + action mapping are thin glue over the tested DB behavior). **Out of scope (deliberate):** retention %/warranty billing Б─■ a finance feature the app resists (status-only at most, per ceo-review); not built. **Project lifecycle now complete:** active/on_hold (full edit) Б├▓ completed (locked for new work; warranty: defects reopen individual WPs to rework Б├▓ fix Б├▓ re-approve) Б├▓ archived; reopen the project via statusБ├▓active. **Audit-found project-status gap closed.**
